  sl          
 sīhaḷavatthūpakaraṇaṃ 
 namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa 
  
     tissatunnavāyassa vatthu  
  
 evamanusuyyate  sīhaḷadīpe kira   anurādhapure tisso nāma tunnavāyo sibbanakammena jīvati  tisaraṇagato pañcasikkhāpadiko  saddho pasanno buddhasāsane attano sarīraṃ kāḷasuttakena phāletvā   sibbanakammaṃ karoti  aḍḍhasarīraṃ me mātāpitunaṃ hotu  aḍḍhaṃ mayhaṃti    so suriye uṭṭhite   yāva majjhantikasamayā kammaṃ karonto yaṃ yaṃ labhati  taṃ taṃ bhikkhusaṃghassa datvā majjhantikato yāva suriyatthaṃgamā yaṃ yaṃ labhati tena tena mātāpitaro poseti  so divase divase dānaṃ dento kadāci dasantaṃ  vīsāya  tiṃsāya  cattālīsāya  paññāsāya  satānaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ kadāci bahukānaṃ pi bhattaṃ deti  cīvarādikaṃ ca deti  evaṃ jīvamānaṃ naṃ mātāpitaro evaṃ yācanti  
    karoma te gharāvāsaṃ  narānaṃ   esā dhammatā  
 sarīraṃ jagganatthāya  yā sā tuyhaṃ bhavissati  
 tisso bhaṇati  
   antarāyakarā esā dhammājīvassa   jantuno 
 dānasīlarataṃ cittaṃ gharāvāsena natthiko     sallaṃ saṃgo ca paṃko ca gaṇḍo rogo bhayaṃ iti parivajjeti taṃ sādhu kusalo antarāyikaṃ  
  
  sl          
  
    andhakaraṇaṃti taṃ vuttaṃ acakkhukaraṇaṃti ca 
 aññāṇakaraṇaṃ idaṃ  paññā tattha nirujjhati  
    sutampi nassati ettha  sīlaṃpi paridhaṃsati  
 hirottappaṃ vināseti  mittadhammona tiṭṭhati    ākāsagamane siddhā pañcābhiññā mahiddhikā 
 jhānalābhī mahesakkhā appesakkhā tahiṃ ahuṃ  
    te vā tatopi   aññepi kāmesu dosadassino 
 parivajjiṃsu te kāme visaṃca jīvitatthikā 
    acchādanaṃ ābharaṇaṃ annaṃ pānaṃ vilepanaṃ 
 sadā naṃ paribhuñjanti itthinaṃ natthi tittatā    yadi me bhariyā hoti esā puttānamāgamo  
 puttadārapamattassa kusalattaṃ na tiṭṭhati  
     chaḍḍetvā kusalaṃ kammaṃ    kāmesu ce pamajjati 
 viddhaṃsetvāna saddhammaṃ pacchā tappati dummati 
     iti dose samekkhitvā gharāvāsenanatthiko 
 mamantaraṃ ca tumhākaṃ mātugāmo navijjati  
     evaṃ vākyaṃ nisāmetvā tissassa pitumātaro 
 anattikoti ñatvāna tuṇhībhūtā tadā ahuṃ  
     so gharāvāsanicchanto brahmacāraṃ samācari  
 tassa sampannasīlassa kittisaddo abbhuggato  
     anurādhapure tisso seṭṭho ca sīlavāti ca  
 sasarīraṃ vibhajitvā ahū so gurupūjakoti  
  
 tadā khīṇāsavā bhikkhū tusitapuraṃ gantvā dve vimānāni samūkhāni disvā deve pucchanti  devā bhaṇanti  
     rañño ca saddhātissassa  tissassa tunnavāyassa    
 ete ṭhitā dūve vyamhā sajālā sampaṭimukhāti  
  taṃ  sutvā te bhikkhu anurādhapuraṃ ganatvā manussānaṃ arocesuṃ manussā saddhātissarañño nivedesuṃ  rājā tunnavāyaṃ pakkosāpetvā paṭipucchi  evaṃ cevaṃ ca karosīti  evaṃ devāti  mayhaṃ bhāgaṃ dehī ti  
  
  sl          
  
 demi    deva  tuyhaṃ bhāgaṃ sabbasattānaṃ cāti  rājā attano makuṭaṃ tassa adāsi  attano pāsādassa purato pāsādavaramekaṃ suvaṇṇarajatādiupakaraṇasampannaṃ adāsi  samākulaṃ catupaṇṇāsavatthasahassāni sahassuṭṭhānakaṃ janapadamekaṃ ca adāsi tunnavāyo mahādānapati ahosi  tato paṭṭhāya bhikkhusaṃghassa cīvarādīni na dullabhāni honti  tassa maraṇakāle dhammaṃ asuṇitvā vippalapatīti āhaṃsu  guṇakittite  
  
     rāja  nāhaṃ vilapāmi devatā turitayanti maṃ 
 tāsāhaṃ lapayi     bhante  āgamethāti abraviṃ  
     yāvatā tambapaṇṇiyaṃ vasanti jinasāvakā  
 ticivarāni sabbesaṃ nikkhattuṃ ca adāsahaṃ 
     sahassakkhattuṃ dīpānaṃ sahassaṃ jālitāni    me 
 akāladhammasavaṇaṃ sahassaṃ ca pavattitaṃ  
     madhuṃ ghataṃ ca telaṃ ca phāṇitaṃ osadhāni ca 
 bahūni bahuso dinnā dāni kiṃ vilapāmahaṃ  
     pariyante kataṃ kāraṃ toseti dadato    manaṃ 
 buddhe dhamme ca saṃghe ca tīsu vatthusu nissitaṃ 
     bahuṃ hi kusalaṃ katvā sakyasīhassa sāsane pītisomanassaṃ āsi tāso mayhaṃ na vijjati  
  
     rathaparivāritaturitā mamekaṃ 
 chapi ca devagaṇā samāgatā  
     paṭhaviyaṃ gati  bhaddakaṃ pasatthaṃ     bhagavati pāraṃgato brūhetha me     
  aññattha evaṃ dissati   
      kimica hi tahiṃ bhaddakaṃ pasatthaṃ     bhagavati hirigatā brahmeva me  
  
  sl          
  
     jinavaraṃgadaha  pamādahīnaṃ 
 bahusaddhammakathaṃ tahiṃ pavattaṃ 
 tusitapuravaraṃ gatasugataṃ 
 sugatamado muni aṃkuro bhāsoti  
  aññavatthusmiṃ evaṃ dissati   
     pavararathagaṇā samāgatā te 
 mama puratova surālayā idāni 
 kimivahi tahiṃ bhaddakaṃ pasatthaṃ     
 bhagavati hirigatā brahmeva me     
     purīva arahānaṃ pamādavajje     
 bahulaṃ dhammakathā sadā pavattā 
 tusitavare deve subhaddakamhī ajitavaro muniaṃkuro ca tattha  
     iti bahu kusalāni sañcayitvā 
 jinavarasāsanaṃ pavaraṃ labhitvā 
 tusitapurarathavaramāruhitvā 
 pavanapathena    payāti tunnavāyo      yaṃ kiṃci kusalaṃ kammaṃ suddhacittassa jantuno 
 abhiṇhaṃ sevamānassa uttamatthaṃ ca pūrati  
     tunnavāyaṃ ca disvāna ye puññaṃ nappamajjare 
 te pasādaṃ janessanti dhammapītissa bhikkhuno  
     akusalamevaṃ vajjayitvā 
 kusalapathaṃ yadi sevatī sadā 
 amitasukhasampadaṃ ca bhutvā 
 ariyasukhaṃ labhate yathāsukhenāti  
  
 tu nna vā ya va tthu pa ṭha maṃ 
  
     a k   sīhaḷadīpato      a   sarīraṃguṭṭhaṃ suttakaṃ  
     a   pāpetvā      k  mayhaṃ hotu      k   uṭṭhite sūriye 
     k     k   tanūnaṃ    dhammajīvissa 
     a   devādayopi      dhammaṃ      a h  tissatunnavāyassaca      a h   potthakesu natthi      k h   ṭhapasiṃ       a k  jalayisu 
      k   dāyako      k a  gaganapathena 
     haritālatissavatthu  
  
  sl          
 evamanusuyyate sīhaḷadīpe anurādhapurassa paccimadisāyaṃ pañcayojanamatte samuddappadese bhumaṃgaṇo nāma gāmo atthi  tasmiṃ gāme vāhasahassabhatikulaṃ   atthi  tasmiṃ kule gharaṇiyā satta puttā arogā balavanto tesu jeṭṭhakā cha janā kammaṃ karonti tesaṃ kaṇiṭṭho tisso nāma dārako kiñci na karoti  te chajanā mātuyā khiyyanti  amma  tisso kiṃci na karotī ti  mātā bhaṇati  hotu tāva  idāni tisso taruṇo kīḷāpasuto  pacchā cattānaṃ jānitvā kammaṃ karissatī ti  so kamena vaḍḍhitvā soḷasavassuddesiko jāto tassa mātāpitaro attano samānakulassa vāhasahassabhati kulassa sumanaṃ nāma dārikaṃ ānetvā tissadārakena saddhiṃ vivāhaṃ akaṃsu tadā kirassa mātā suṇhāya pañca dhanāni adāsi  nāḷitaṇḍulaṃ  mūsalaṃ  udukkhalaṃ  pidhānena saha ghaṭaṃ  bhuñjanakabhājanaṃti  datvā attanā visuṃ vasāpesi  dārikā tāni disvā ekamante nisīditvā rodati  tisso āgantvā bhariyaṃ rodantiṃ disvā bhadde  kasmā roda sīti  sā sabbaṃ tassa ācikkhi  so bhaṇati  bhadde  
  
    mādisaṃ purisaṃ laddhā sumane kissa rodasi  
 karitvā purisakāraṃ te pūrayissāmi mānasaṃ  
    mā ca tvaṃ sumane soci  mā bhāyi ca bhaddake 
 mamatthi porisaṃ puññaṃ nāma dhavānurūpato  
 so evaṃ vatvā puna āha  tena hi sumane suve nāḷitaṇaḍulaṃ dvebhāgaṃ katvā ekaṃ saṃghassa salākabhattaṃ pavāhi ekaṃ amhe dve janā bhuñjissāmāti vihāraṃ ganatvāsvātanāya saṃghato  ekaṃ bhikkhuṃ   bhattaggaṃ nimantesi  taṃ bhattaggaṃ saṃgho daharasāmaṇeraṃ pāpesi  dārako taṃ labhitvā haṭṭhatuṭṭho suve vāhasahassabhatikulaputtassa tissassa paṭhamasalākabhattaṃ paṇītaṃ labhissāmīti 
  sl          
  
 kālassevassa gharaṃ gato  sumanāpi loṇakapaṇṇena   saha bhattaṃ tassa adāsi  sāmaṇero taṃ gahetvā dummano āsanasālāyaṃ gato sabbe sāmaṇerā saṃgamma passiṃsu passitvā sabbe hasitvā tissaṃ ḍākaloṇa tisso ti   nāmaṃ akaṃsu  sāmaṇeropi taṃ bhattaṃ sumanāya purato yeva āsanasālāya dāruvatiyantarena chaḍḍesi  sumanā gharaṃ gantvā rodi  tisso āgantvā bhadde kasmā rodasī ti pucchi  sāmi  tumhaṃ bhattaṃ mayhaṃ purato yeva so sāmaṇero āsanasālāya dāruvatiyantare chaḍḍesi sabbe sāmaṇerā hasitvā tuyhaṃ nāmaṃ ḍākaloṇakatissoti akaṃsūti  tisso aho sundaraṃ ācariyānaṃ kataṃ nāmaṃ  matthakena sampaṭicchāmi  mayhaṃ nāmaṃ sakalatambapaṇṇidīpe pākaṭaṃ bhavissati  mā ukkaṇṭhīti vatvā pātova lāyaṃ gahetvā khettaṃ gantvā bhatiyā dhaññaṃ lāyi  so balavā sīghaṃ lāyi bahuṃ lāyitvā manussānaṃ cittaṃ ārādhesi  te tuṭṭhā majjhantike yeva ammaṇadhaññaṃ adaṃsu  so taṃgahetvā gharaṃ netvābhariyāya adāsi  bhadde iminā kiṇitvā maccha  maṃsa  dadhi sappisampayuttaṃ paṇītaṃ bhattaṃ katvā dehīti vatvā puna khettaṃ gato lāyituṃ ārahi  yāva sāyaṇhaṃ lāyitvā ammaṇadhaññaṃ labhitvā agamāsi  evaṃ so kammaṃ katvā bahuṃ dhaññaṃ labhitvā dānaṃ pavattesi tassa bhattikā bhikkhū vaḍḍhanti  kadāci dasa  vīsaṃ  tiṃsaṃ  cattāḷīsaṃ  paññāsaṃ  sataṃ  atirekasataṃti  so dvisū tīsu saṃvaccha resu atikkantesu bhikkhusahassampi dātuṃ samattho  loṇatisso mahādānapatīti sīhaḷadīpe pākaṭo jāto  
  
 so bahunnaṃ dātukāmo bhikkhū alabhanto bhikkhū pucchi   ahambhante bahunnaṃ dātukāmo  na ca bhikkhū 
  
  sl          
  
 labhāmi  kuhiṃ bhikkhū labhissāmī ti  bhikkhū bhaṇanti  upāsaka  nāgadīpaṃ bahū bhikkhū gacchanti bhagavato paribhogasāṭakactiyeṃ vandanatthāya yadi tvaṃ tahiṃ gaccheyyāsi  bahū bhikkhū labheyyāsīti sādhu  bhante  tahiṃ gacchāmīti  so nāgadīpaṃ gantvā haritālagāme bāhubalena   kammaṃkatvā danaṃ labhitvā saddho puññatthiko hutvā paribhogactiyeṃ vandanatthāya āgatāgatāgatānaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ deti  dasannampi vīsatiyāpi yāva sahassānaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ dānaṃ deti  tenassa haritālagāme vasatīti haritālagāmakatissoti nāmaṃ labhi  tattha ekasmiṃ divase navasatā bhikkhū navakkhattuṃ āganatvā tassa piṇḍapātaṃ gaṇhanti  tesaṃ antare tassā yeva rattiyā dve arahantā sahāyakā piyaṃgudīpe nisinnāsamūllāpaṃ karonti  ime hi āvuso dīpā bhikkhūnaṃ lābhagocarā  ayaṃ jambudīpo ca tambapaṇṇidīpo ca 
    dvinnaṃ imesaṃ dīpānaṃ katame dīpavāsikā 
 manussā saddhā pasannā  bhikkhaṃ ca sulabhaṃ kuhiṃ  
  
 tattha eko arahā jambudīpaṃ pasaṃsati eko pana arahā tambapaṇṇiṃ pasaṃsati  
    evaṃ te mantayitvāna svātanāya duve vasī 
 abbhuggantvāna vehāsaṃ otaruṃ dvepi dīpake  
    ṭhite majajhantike kāle bhikkhū bhutvāna niggatā  
 sumanā dvāraṃ nissāya bhikkhuṃ passati sāparaṃ    
    pekkhantī laddhā taṃ   bhikkhuṃ carantaṃ   tattha tattha ca hatthe pattaṃ gahetvāna pāvisī sā sakaṃ gharaṃ  
    taṇḍulampi gahetvāna sappiṃ phāṇiṃ madhuṃ dadhiṃ 
 āharitvāna sā khippaṃ pavitvā guḷasaṃyutaṃ   
    madhuraṃ paṇītaṃ bhattaṃ paripūresi bhājanaṃ  
 pattaṃ ādhārakaṃ katvā gharadvāraṃ pavattitaṃ  
  
  sl          
  
    thero pattamagahetvā  thero sumanambravi  
 pattaṃ   muñca sumane naṃ  gacchissaṃ yena patthitaṃ  
     nāhaṃ deva pamuñcāmi  natthi me tādisaṃ balaṃ 
 tumhe pattaṃ gahetvāna gacchatha yena patthitaṃ  
     pattaṃ gahetvā so thero gaccanto ambare tadā 
 pekkhantiyāva sumanāya so vasī gaganaṃ gato  
     ṭhitā dvāre ca sumanā haṭṭhatuṭṭhā katañjalī vasī so pekkhamānāya yāva dīpaṃ pavissati    
     āgantvā bhikkhusaṃghassa paripūri yadicchakaṃ 
 pūrayampi sahassānaṃ pariyantaṃ na dissati  
     bhuñjitvā pariyosāne sabbesu pattadhovite 
 jambudīpaṃ samāgantvā pacchā so āgato vasī 
  
 tadā ca haritālatissassa vaṇṇaṃ vaṇṇayantā sabbe bhikkhū nisīdanti  cattāro ca lokapālā loke anu vicarantā pekkhanti  te sabbaṃ dīṭṭhaṃ suvaṇṇapaṭṭelikhitvā devānaṃ tāvatiṃsānaṃ sudhammāya sabhāya vācenti  
  
     tassa gāmassa nāmena tisso so haritālako 
 guṇehi pākaṭo eso sakalāya tambapaṇṇiyaṃ  
     ediso sīlasampanno saddhodānapatī ca so 
 na cireneva kālena devakāyaṃ gamissatīti  
  
 taṃ sutvā sakko devānamindo vimbhito vīmaṃsāya cittaṃ uppadesi tisso ce saddho hoti  udāhu assaddho yadi saddho hoti  bhikkhūnaṃ santike pasādaṃ karissati yadi saddho na hoti  appasādaṃ karissatīti bhikkhuvesaṃ gahetvā haritālatissassa gharaṃ agamāsi  tasmiṃ khaṇe subyañjanaṃ bhojanaṃ tassa purato ṭhapetvā pānīyathālakaṃ gahetvā ṭhitāya sumanāya sakko tassa santikaṃ gantvā āha  
  
     upāsaka mahātissa  maṃ uttārehi sāgarā 
 anurādhapuraṃ gantvā namassāmi ca cetiyaṃ  
  
  sl          
     sādhu bhante ti so tuṭṭho uṭṭhahitvāna āsanā 
 abhuñjitvāna bhojanaṃ taṃ bhikkhuṃ anubandhayi  
     titthaṃ patvāna so bhikkhu tissassa idamabravi  
 ghare te me mahātissa  pamuṭṭhaṃ dakasāṭakaṃ  
     tattheva te nivattitvā gharaṃ gantvā ubho janā 
 dakasāṭakamādāya puna titthaṃ upāgatā 
     upagantvāna taṃ titthaṃ puna tissaṃ idabravi  ghare te me mahātissa  pamuṭṭhaṃ daṇḍakaṃ mayā  
     tattheva so nivattitvā gharaṃ gantvā ubho janā 
 tattha daṇḍakamādāya puna titthaṃ upāgatā  
     upagantvā nadītitthaṃ   puna tissaṃ idabravi  
 ghare te me mahātissa  pamuṭṭhā telanāḷikā  
     tatheva te nivattitvā gharaṃ gantvā ubho janā 
 telanāḷikamādāya puna titthaṃ upāgatā 
     upagantvā nadī titthaṃ   puna tissaṃ idabravi  
 ghare te me mahātissa  pamuṭṭhaṃ kāyabandhanaṃ  
     tattheva te nivattitvā gharaṃ gatā   ubho janā  
 sasarīraṃ hi dassetvā tissaṃ so idamabravi     sudukkaraṃ kataṃ tissa  hiṇḍanto sabbarattiyaṃ 
 saddho ca dāyako cāsi vīmaṃsatthāyi dhāgatoti  
 tisso āha  
     na mayhaṃ dukkaraṃ etaṃ purisassa arogino 
 aññampi tādisaṃ kammaṃ purisānaṃ sukhāvahaṃ    
     mayhaṃ upaṭṭhitā esā sumanā dukkaraṃ kari  
 dakathālaṃ gahetvāna aṭṭhāsi sabbarattiyaṃ  sakko āha  
     tuyhaṃ bhariyā yoggā   yassā tvaṃ tissa sāmiko  
 sameti tuyhaṃ saṃvāso devo viya ca nandane  
     āpucchāmi mahātissa  gacchissaṃ nandanaṃ vanaṃ 
 vīmaṃsanatthaṃ āgacchiṃ  saddho vā so asaddhako 
  
  sl           
     haritālassa gāmassa samuddassa ca antare 
 yojanaṃ parihāpetvā devarājā divaṃ gatoti  
 vatthu vitthāretabbaṃ  
     iti bahukusalāni saṃvayitvā 
 jinavarasāsanasampadaṃ labhitvā 
 tusitapurarathaṃ   samāruhitvā 
 gaganapathena payāti tissanāmoti  
  
 haritālatissavatthu dutiyaṃ

      k h   bhavissati       b h k   ntvāna taṃ titthaṃ

      h k   payogā       b b k   tusitavararataṃ 
  metteyya vatthu  
  
 eva manusuyyate  tambapaṇṇidīpe rohaṇajanapade kambojagāme  māleyyattheropaṭivasati  thero pubbaṇhasamayaṃ nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya kambojagāmaṃ piṇḍāya pāvisi  athaññataro puriso aṭṭha uppalahatthake gahetvā gāmaṃpavisanto theraṃ disvā tāni pupphāni adāsi  thero tāni gahetvā cintesi  kuhiṃ āro pessāmi  mahācetiye udāhu cetiyagiripabbate  udāhu mahābodimhīti  putassa etadahosi  yaṃ nūnāhaṃ bhagavato dakkhiṇadāṭhaṃ ca cūḷāmaṇicetiyaṃ ca tāvatiṃsa bhavane pūjessāmīti  cintetvā taṃ khaṇaññeca vehāsaṃ abbhuggantvā accharāsaṃghātamattena vejayanta pāsādassa pamukhe aṭṭhāsi nīluppalakalāpe gahetvā sakko devānamindo bhagavato dakkiṇadāṭhaṃ ca kesadhātu yo ca cūlāmaṇissa abbhantare pakkhipitvā vejayanta pāsādassa purato tiyojanaparimaṇḍalaṃ cetiyaṃ patiṭṭhā pesi  thero taṃ cetiyaṃ upasaṃkamitvā aṭṭhasu ṭhānesu abhivādetvā padakkhiṇaṃ katvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi  sakko theraṃ disvā saparivāro āgantvā abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi  thero sakkaṃ pucchi  sakka devānaminda  
  
  sl           
  
 metteyyo bodhisatto idhāgamissatīti  āma bhante  ajjaṭṭhamī āgamissati  so hi pakkhassa pañcamiyaṃ aṭṭhamiyaṃ cātuddasiyaṃ paṇṇarasiyaṃ ca vandanatthāya āgacchatevā ti  evaṃ tesaṃ kathentānaṃ yeva pācīnapasse mahatā parivārena eko devaputto dissati   taṃ disvā thero  devarājaṃ pucchi  eso metteyyo bodhisattoti  sakko  neso bodhisatto  so aññataro deva puttoti āha  thero  katamo esoti  sakko āha  
  
    anurādhapure pubbe sūcikammena jīvati 
 bahupuññakaro eso tunnavāyoti vissuto  
 so devaputto āgantvā dakkhiṇadisāyaṃ aṭṭhāsi  upasobhayamāno  puna eko devaputto tatheva mahatā parivārena āgacchi  thero devarājaṃ pucchi sakko neso bodhisatto  aññataro devaputtoti  katamo esoti  sakko āha  
  
    haritālamahāgāme mahādānapatī ahu  
 haritālakatissoti  sopi āgacchate idhāti  
 so devaputto āgantvā pacchimāya disāya upasobhaya māno aṭṭhāsi  puna eko devaputto tatheva mahatā parivārena āgacchati  taṃ disvā thero devarājānaṃ pucchi sakko  neso bodhisatto  aññataro devaputtoti  katamo esoti  sakko āha  
    dūṭṭhagāmaṇīabhayassa kaṇiṭṭho so mahāyaso 
 saddhātissoti nāmena  so pi āgacchate idha so devaputto āgantvā uttaradisāya upasobhaya māno aṭṭhāsi puna eko devaputto tassa pacchato tatheva mahatā parivārena āgacchati taṃ disvā devarājānaṃ pucchi  sakko neso bodhisatto aññataro deva puttoti  thero katamo esoti  sakko āha  
  
  sl           
  
    tathāgatassa yo thūpaṃ kārayī dīpapajjare     duṭṭhagāmiṇī abhayo sopi āgacchate idhāti  
  
 so devaputto āgantvā pūrimāya disāya upasobhayamāno aṭṭhāsi  tesaṃ pacchato metteyyo bodhisatto āgacchati  tassa catusu passesu catasso devakaññāyā saparivārāyo alaṃkatāyo āgacchanti paramattakāyā  jalitaggisannibhā  tā devakaññāyo disvā thero devarājānaṃ pucchi  etā catasso vanitā manussaloke kiṃ puññaṃ akaṃsūti  tāsu ekā vicitra vaṇṇā vicitraraṃsā  vicitrālaṃkārā  vicitravatthā  ekā rattaraṃsā rattālaṃkārā  rattavatthā ekā tambapīta vaṇṇā  tambapītaraṃsā  tambapītālaṃkārā  tambapītavatthā ekā pītavaṇṇā  pītaraṃsā  pītālaṃkārā  pītavatthāti  devarājā bhaṇati  
    raṭṭhassuṭṭhānakālamihī kumbhakārassa gāmake 
 citrapupphehi pūjetvā sā devi dakkhṇe ṭhitā  
    nāgadīpamhi sā therī yācitvā uppalaṃ sayaṃ 
 cetiyaṃ abhipūjesi vāmapasse ca sā ṭhitā  
    laṃkāya janapadamhi kaṇṇikārakagāmake 
 pūjetvā kaṇikārehi pacchā sā dakkhiṇe ṭhitā  
    tamhā passena yo pubbe āsi tammaṇagāmake  
 pūjaṃ lohaketuṃ  katvā pacchā vāmena sā ṭhitā  
    anekadevaputtā pi devakaññāpi yā piyā 
 tā metteyyaṃ parivāretvā gacchanti tāva ambare  
     puṇṇamāyaṃ yathā cando saradakāleva bhānumā 
 vaṇṇarūpena tejena devamajjhe virocati  
     migamajjhe yathā sīho  gavamajjhe yathūsabho  
 nagamajejha yathā meru  devamajjhe virocati      pakkhimajjheva garuḷo  nadīmajjheva sāgaro tarumajjhe pāriccatto  devamajjhe virocati  
  
  sl           
  
     pupphamajjhe kokanado  maṇimajjhe veḷuriyo  
 naramajjhe cakkavattī  devamajjhe virocati  
     pabbatagge yathā aggi  suvaṇṇakaṇṇikā yathā 
 sabbe deve atikkamma vaṇṇatejena dippati 
     evaṃ anomavaṇṇo so metteyyo jinapuṃgavo  
 sabbadevagaṇamajjhe pajjalantova āgato 
  
 tā vatasso devakaññāyo yāvajīvaṃ manussaloke mālādihi pūjaṃ katvā tato cutā tusitabhavane nibbattā anekasataparivārā bodhisattaṃ parivāretvā āgantvā tiyojanaparimaṇḍalaṃ cūlamaṇicetiyaṃ vanditvā padakkhiṇaṃ katvā yena māleyyatthero tena gantvā māleyyattheraṃ vanditvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhaṃsu  metteyyo bodhisatto māleyyattheraṃ pucchi  kuto bhante āgacchathā ti  jambudīpā mahārājāti  kiṃ bhante jambudīpakānaṃ manussānaṃ sambhāraṃnti  atthi sambhāraṃ mahārājāti  kiṃ bhante sambhāranti  
  
     yaṃ kiñci kusalaṃ katvā tuyhaṃ patthenti bodhiyā 
 metteyyasammāsambuddhassa dassanaṃ bhavatu no sadā ti  
 bodhisatto āha  
     yaṃ kiñci kusalaṃ katvā mamaṃ patthentī mānusā 
 saṃsārabhayabhītānaṃ bhavāmi bhavamocako  
     avijjābhavanaṃ ghoraṃ taṇhājālasamākulaṃ 
 vuyhantaṃ vaturoghehi lokaṃ santārayissahaṃ 
     kilesāvaṭṭapakkhante  taṇhātakkarasevite 
 saṃsāranadīsamūḷhe sumaggaṃ dassayissahaṃ  
     saṃjīve kālasutte ca tāpane mahā tāpane 
 avīciniraye satte  sabbe  nibbāpayissaha  
     aññāṇabandhanā baddhe taṇhājālavasaṃ  gate 
 chetvāna bandhanaṃ sabbe sampāpessāmi nibbutiṃ  
      micchādiṭṭhikavāṭe hi dvāsaṭṭhidiṭṭhiaggale 
 maggaṃgamaggatāḷehi  vivarissāmi pāṇinaṃ  
  
  sl           
  
     rāgadosatamandhānaṃ  hatanettānajantunaṃ 
 paññāsalākaṃ datvāna nayanaṃ sodhayissahaṃ 
     sokāturaṃ dukkhitaṃ ca  jarāmaraṇapīḷitaṃ 
 ñāṇosadhavaraṃ datvā tikicchissāmi  pāṇinaṃ 
     mohandhakārasammuḷhe cāresu caramānuse  
 ñāṇālokaṃ karitvāna vivarissāmi taṃ gharaṃ   
      apāye parivattantaṃ atāṇamaparāyanaṃ 
 upāyā uddharitvāna dassayissaṃ    parāyananti  
      bhikkhunīdūsakā bhikkhū  santi saṃghassa bhedakā  
 pañcānantariyaṃ kammaṃ thūpabodhīna bhedakaṃ 
     bodhisattassa māraṇaṃ maccherā ca musāvādā 
 na honti mama santike  manussalokaṃ gantvāna 
 mayā kathita me ve taṃ vadeyyāthāti pāṇinaṃ ti 
  
 idaṃ vatvā metteyyo bodhisattā theraṃ vanditvā tusitabhavanaṃ paccāgato  theropinivattitvā tambapaṇṇidīpaṃ sampāpuṇi  thero kambojagāmaṃ piṇḍāya pāvisi  tato paṭṭhāya ñātakānaṃ ārocesi  ñātakāpi therassa ovādaṃ sutvā sabbāni tāni kusalakammāni kariṃsu  te manussā āyupariyosāne manussalokato cavitvā devalokaṃ sampāpuṇiṃsūti   
  
     asaṃkheyyāni dveaṭṭha saṃvayitvā kusalaṃ bahuṃ 
 gantvā ñāṇaparipākaṃ sambodhiṃ pāpuṇissati  
     pāpuṇitvāna sambodhiṃ anukampāya pāṇinaṃ dhammanāvamadhiṭṭhāya tāressati   sadevakaṃ  
     taṃ dhammanāvamāruyha dhammapītissa bhikkhuno 
 saṃsārasmābhinikkhamma hoti nibbāṇapatti sā 
     viseso tu mahāsatto bhavissati anāgate 
 metteyyasammāsambuddho saraṇo sabbapāṇinaṃti  
 metteyyavatthu tatiyaṃ 
  
      h   kammojagāme     k   āgacchati 
     b  parapattakāyā     k   kasikammakagāmake 
     k   lokaketuṃ  b  dhaṃlodake  
     b   tatte      b   satte 
     h   taṇhāvālavasaṃ      h   rāgadosamohandhānaṃ

 dissanti

  mahādatta vatthu  
  
 evamanusuyyate  tambapaṇṇidīpe rohaṇajanapade aññataro sākaṭiko  so guḷabharītaṃ  sakaṭaṃ ādāya gambhīrakaddamaṃ patto  sakaṭo kaddamamajjhe laggo  taseseko mahādatto nāma balivaddo kaḍḍhituṃ na sakkoti  sākaṭiko evamāha  
  
    gambhīre kaddame ajja uddhareyya tuvaṃ yadi  
 yuge puna na yojessaṃ evaṃ jānāhi dattaka  
 taṃ sutvā mahādatto ussāhaṃ parivattamāno  daḷhaṃ parakkamaṃ katvā uddharituṃ ussāhamakāsi sākaṭiko balivaddaṃ parāmasitvā pājesi  balivaddopi sabbathāmena sakaṭaṃ dhāresi evaṃ chavāre alikaṃ bhaṇantopi uttarāpesi   puna sattamavāre sampatte balivaddo sūṭṭhu parakkamaṃ karontāpi na sakkoti  jiṇṇadubbalabhāvena puna vegena kaḍḍhantassa uraṃ bhijji  so lohitaṃ vamitvā tatthe va pati  so taṃ chaḍḍetvā aññaṃ yojetvā pakkāmi  aññataro kumbhakāro āgantvā tassa jīvantasseva cammaṃ uppāṭetvā mattikāmaddanatthāya gato  aññataro gandhabbo āgantvā nahārūni phāletvā gahetvā gato  vīṇātantikaraṇatthāya  puna eko luddako sunakhehi saha āgantvā maṃsaṃ chinditvā sunakhānaṃ adāsi  sunakhāpi maṃsāni mukhena luñcitvā khāditvā pakkamanti  jīvantasseva kāyaṃ kaṇhakipillikā  khādanti  so mahādukkhappatto nipajji  
  
 tadā cūlapiṇḍapātikatissatthero pañcahi bhikkhusatehi saddhiṃ tena maggena gacchanto taṃ balivaddaṃ disvā kāruññaṃ uppādetvā pattena udakaṃ āharāpetvā pāyesi  goṇopi yāvadatthaṃ pivitvā assāsaṃ labhi thero tassa purato nisīditvā mahāsatipaṭṭhānasuttaṃ bhāsitvā 
  
  sl           
 saraṇe adāsi  silāni therassa diyyamānassa goṇo kālaṃkaronto dhamme nimittaṃ gahetvā tāvatiṃsabhavane tiṃsayojanike kanakavimāne uppanno accharāsahassa parivuto  pubbajātiṃ passitvā therassa kaññutaṃ dassetuṃ aḍḍharattasamaye accharāsahassaparivuto saha vimānena āgantvā therassa pādamūle nipatitvāekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi  thero ajānanto viya pucchati  
  
    abhirūpo dassanīyo vaṇṇenobhāsayaṃ disā 
 accharāgaṇasaṃkiṇṇokonu tvamasi mārisa  
 devaputto āha  
    balivaddo pure āsiṃ apāyapaṭisandhiko 
 kusalaṃ nābhijānāmi  mohayonigato ahaṃ  
    gambhīre kaddama  majjhe sakaṭe yojayanti maṃ  
 sakaṭaṃ uddharantassa hadayaṃ me viphālayi  
    uttiṇṇamatte sakaṭe tattheva patito ahaṃ  
 patitaṃ dubbalaṃ disvā  chaḍḍetvā sāmiko gato  
    jīvantameva maṃ keci cammaṃ   maṃsaṃ nahāru ca 
 uppāṭetvāna gacchanti niddayākaruṇā janā  
    evaṃ vyasanamāpannaṃ disvā bhavaṃ mahāmuni 
 satipaṭṭhānasuttantaṃ abhāsi anukampako     suttantapariyosāne  saraṇāni adāsi me 
 silāni  diyyamānassa maraṇaṃ me upaṭṭhitaṃ  
    tattha kālaṃkaritvāna tāvatiṃsūpago  ahaṃ  
 yadi sīlāni dajjeyya yāmaloke bhaveyyahaṃ  
     devalokagatassāpi pubbanāmaṃ na nassati 
 mahādatto ti jānanti sabbe devā saindakā  
     balivaddo ahaṃ santo dukkhappatto sudāruṇaṃ 
 vatvā subhāsitaṃ suttaṃ saraṇaṃ ca adāsi me      sotadvāraṃ paviṭṭhassa phalaṃ passāmi īdisaṃ  
 mameva parivārentā sahassā accharā imā  
 taṃ hi suttaṃ nisāmetvā pattomhi īdisaṃ siriṃ  
  sl           
  
     ye janā itthiyo  kāle sāsanaṃ payirupāsare  
 tesaṃ vattabbakaṃ natthi pattānaṃ sukhamuttamaṃ  
     datvā saraṇasīlānī taṃ suttaṃ yeva bhāsatha taṃ dhammanāvamāruyha tārehi maṃ bhavaṇṇavā  
     tassa suttassa tejena sīlena saraṇena ca 
 apāyadehaṃ chetvāna devadehaṃ labhiṃ ahaṃ   
     evaṃ so yācī taṃ  theraṃ satipaṭṭhānadesanaṃ 
 devaputto mahādatto viratto bhavasandhiyā  
     saraṇāni ca sīlāni datvā thero mahavasī 
 taṃ yeva suttaṃ desetvā vineti paṭhame phale  
     so dhammacakkhuṃ laddhāna buddhaputtassa santike 
 sirasā onamitvāna pādosu paṇamaṃ kari  
     sahassaaccharā saddhiṃ sotāpattiphale ṭhito 
 gagane haṃsarājāva pakkamī so surālayaṃ  
     tasmā sujanasaṃsaggaṃ pasaṃsanti tathāgatā  
 taṃ sutvā dhammapītiṃ ca bhiyyo bhiyyo paṃsaṃsati  
     bahuguṇajananaṃ ti hi ñatvā dhīro 
 sujanānaṃ yo samāgame pasaṃseyya     
 asuramiva bahuṃ ca tādisaṃ labhitvā     
 tathāvidhaṃ     sappurisaṃ seveyyāti  
  
 mahādattavatthu chaṭṭhaṃ      
  
      h  sotullabharitaṃ     h   ussāha parigattamano 
     h   uddharāpesi     kutthakipillikā  
    tāvatiṃsagato      k   vitthiyo    vā itthiyo   
    yācati  
     manorammaṃsavatthu   
  
 evamanusuyyate  anurādhapure aññataro daharasāmaṇero upajjhāyassa piṇḍapātaṃ bhuñjantassa kusuma paṇṇāni  datvā paṇidhānaṃ kari  
  
    iminā puññena me bhante cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca yattha yatthupapajjāmi  mayūramaṃsaṃ samijjhatutī  
  
  sl           
  
 so kālaṃkatvā tasmiṃ yeva nagare aññatarasmiṃ kule uppanno  tassa jātadivasato paṭṭhāya tasmiṃ ghare sadāva mayūramaṃsaṃ uppajjati  tenassa manoramamayūramaṃso ti nāmaṃ kataṃ  so kamena vaḍhḍhitvā agārasmā anagāriyaṃ pabbaji  tassāpi mayūramaṃsaṃ yeva upaṭṭhāsi  ekadivasaṃ aññataro amaccomayūramaṃsaṃ labhitvā manoramaṃ  theraṃ nimantetvā gharaṃ netvā  āsane nisīdāpetvā bhojanaṃ dāpesi bhariyā panassa maṃsalobhena thokaṃ dātukāmā hoti  thokaṃ gaṇhantiyā sabbaṃ upaṭṭhahi  sā viyojetuṃ asakkontī sabbaṃ therassa chupi     taṃ disvā manoramamayūramaṃsatthero sitaṃ pātukaroti  amacco therassa sitakāraṇaṃ pucchanto  
  
    sīlavanto pabbajitā chaḷindriyesu saṃvutā 
 passitvā kāraṇaṃ kiñci sitaṃ pātukaronti te   
    manoramaṃ maṃsaṃ disvā sitaṃ pātukataṃ tayā 
 tamahaṃ sotumicchāmi  brūhi me sitakāraṇaṃ  
 thero āha  
  
     mama puññaṃ  ajānantī thokaṃ sā dātumicchati  
 taṃ sabbaṃ patitaṃ disvā sitaṃ pātukataṃ mayā  
    anavasesaṃ na te denti ye janā maccharī idha 
 puññavantaṃ naraṃ disvā maccharantena tibbarā     
     yādisaṃ me kataṃ puññaṃ dakkhiṇeyyesu tādisu  
 taṃ puññaṃ ajja paccakkhaṃ  antaraṃ sā gavesati  
    maccheranāriṃ disvāna sitaṃ pātukataṃ mayā  
 taṃ kāraṇaṃ vijānāhi aññaṃ mā tvaṃ vikappayi  
  
 amacco therassa puññaṃ passissāmīti punadivase nimantetvā kaṇājakaṃ bilaṃgadutiyaṃ bhariyaṃ āṇāpetvā bahi gato  nagarapāladevatā manussavesena madhuraṃ mayūramaṃsaṃ sālitaṇḍūlaṃ dadhighaṭaṃ ca tassa  bhariyāya datvā idamabravi   
  
  sl           
  
    idaṃ mayūramaṃsaṃ ca taṇḍulaṃ ca dadhīghaṭaṃ 
 amacco pesayī ayye  pacitvā dehi bhikkhunoti 
 amaccabhariyā taṃ sabbaṃ disvā cintesi  
  
    amacco maṃ nivāretvā bahi so niggato tadā 
 puna  tādisāni disvā  pasanno me matipuṇṇeti      
     sādhukaṃ sampaṭicchitvā mayūramaṃsaṃ dadhīghaṭaṃ 
 odanaṃ supacitvāna therassa paṭipādayi  
     āgantvāna tato thero nisīditvāva āsane 
 taṃ bhattaṃ paribhuñjitvā pakkamī yena patthitaṃ  
     so amacco gharaṃ gantvā bhariyaṃ paṭipucchati  
 yaṃ āṇattaṃ mayā sabbaṃ kataṃ te taṃ kaṇājakaṃ  
     sā tassa vacanaṃ sutvā amaccaṃ idamabravi  
 pubbe aññaṃ bhaṇitvāna pacchā aññaṃ pavattitaṃ  
 amacco āha kiṃ mayā punavuttaṃ ti  sā āha  
     yaṃ tayā pesitaṃ sabbaṃ sāliṃ maṃsaṃ dadhiṃ ghataṃ 
 pacitvā sukataṃ bhattaṃ taṃ pādaṃ garusāmikaṃ  
     idaṃ sutvā amacco so vimbhito ca tadā ahu  
 pasādaṃ vipulaṃ katvā vacībheda mudīrayī  
     aho sudesito dhammo buddhenādiccabandhunā 
 upakārāni puññāni agāriyanagārinaṃ  
     kusalaṃ tena kattabbaṃ kusaleneva jantunā  
 mayuramaṃsaṃ disvāna paccakkhaṃ phalamīdisaṃ  
     kaṇājakaṃ bilaṃgena āṇāpetvā gato ahaṃ 
 sāliṃ mayūramaṃsaṃ ca devatā gharamānayi  
     tadā amacco mudito mahādānapatī ahū  
 dhammapītissa dhammante  katabbaṃ kusalaṃ bahūṃ  
     iti naranarāsahassa tissarañño 
 tusitapuramhī gatassa amaccaseṭṭho 
 idha bahu kusalāni saṃcayitvā 
 tusitapuravarameva gato cavitvā  
 manoramamaṃsavatthu sattamaṃ  
  
     mayūramaṃsaṃ          h  upaṭṭhāti  
     h k   manorama mayūramaṃsaṃ      b h   natthi  
     h   pātukarosi tvaṃ     b k h   paccattaṃ  
     h   therameva  tipuṇṇeti      h   dhammavante  
  
  sl           
  
     phussadevattheravatthu  
  
 evamanusuyyate  ariyavaradīpavaṭaṃsake sīhaḷadīpe kālakandaravihāro nāma padhānikavihāro atthi  tasmiṃ vihāre yuttayohī mettā vihārī vattasampanno sāsaneṭhitako phussadevo nāma mahāthero pañcannaṃ bhikkhu satānaṃ ovadanto viharati so manussānaṃ piyo manāpo atīva dassanīyo ahosi  yasmiṃ samaye thero piṇḍāya gacchati  tattha khettesu kasikammaṃ karontā manussā theraṃ disvā balivadde muñcitvā theraṃ vanditukāmā āgacchanti  etthantare balivaddā sadāyeva therassa āgamanaṃ pekkantā somanassacittā jātā  tena cittappasādena tāvatiṃsabhavane nibbattīṃsu  atha balivadda pubbā pañcasatadevaputtā sudhammāyaṃ devasabhāyaṃ sannipatitā devarājassa purato pasaṃsantī  
  
    sīlavā guṇasampanno phussadevoti vissuto 
 kāḷakandaraḷeṇamhi vasatī ca visārado 
    appiccho dhūtavādī ca    sabbasattānukampako   
 pavivekarato jhāyī sampajañño samāhito  
    hitaṃ icchati sattānaṃ mettacittena so vasī 
 pharanto sabbasattesu vasatī kāḷakandare  
    manussānaṃ piyo thero amanussānameva ca 
  pihayanti migapakkhī ca  so niccaṃ vanavāsiko   
    evaṃ anantavaṇṇo so phussadevo jitindriyo  
 therassa ānubhāvena labhāmi tidivaṃ gatiṃ  
    balivaddāva hutvāpi sabbe pañcasatā mayaṃ 
 there  pasādaṃ laddhāna devalokaṃ idhāgatā 
    anekā  migapakkhīpi kimaṃga mānusā pana 
 there cittāni tosetvā saggamaggaṃ visodhayuṃ  
    evaṃ bahunnaṃ sukhado sīlavanto susaṃvuto 
 devatānaṃ manussānaṃ  pasūnaṃ migapakkhinaṃti  
  
  sl           
  
 evaṃ kāḷakandaravihāravāsissa phussadevassa  vaṇṇaṃ sutvā devā tāvatiṃsā therassa dassanakāmā devarājaṃ eva māhaṃsu icchāma mayaṃ mārisa phussadevattheraṃ daṭṭhuṃ ti  sakko sādhūti sampaṭicchitvā  seyyathā pi balavā  puriso sammiñjitaṃ vā bāhaṃ pasāreyya  pasāritaṃ vā bāhaṃ sammiñjeyya  eva meva devesu tāvatiṃsesu antarahito kāḷakandara vihāre phussadevattherassa sammūkhā pāturahosi  sakko theraṃ vanditvā ekamantaṃ ṭhito yācati  
  
    devā bhante tāvatiṃsā icchanti tava dassanaṃ 
 gacchāma devalokamhi pītiṃ paṭilabhanti te  
 thero bhaṇati  
     puthujjanohaṃ devinda  iddhi me natthi tādisā  
 samaṃgī iddhiyā yena gaccheyya tidasālayaṃ  
 sakko bhaṇati  
     puthujjanoti jānāmi  natthi sā iddhiyā tava  
 tamahaṃ uggahessāmi  adhivāsehi cakkhumāti

 kāloti  ñatvā tattha gamanaṃ patthesi  sakko pana chakkhattuṃ theraṃ nimantetvā devalokaṃ nesi dhammasavaṇatthāya  
  
 thero ekadivasaṃ bodhiyaṅganaṃ susammaṭṭhaṃ sammajjitvā buddhaguṇaṃ anussaranto añjaliṃ paggahetvā bodhiṃ olokento aṭṭhāsi  atha māro passitvā vicakkhu karaṇāya mahāvātaṃ nimmiṇitvā bodhiyaṃgaṇe kacavaraṃ chaḍḍetvā gato  puna thero sammajjitvā aṭṭhāsi buddhaguṇaṃ anussaranto  puna māro makkaṭo hutvā taṃ taṃ sākhaṃ gahetvā kacavaraṃ akāsi  puna thero sammajjitvā aṭṭhāsi buddhaguṇaṃ anussaranto  puna māro jiṇṇabalivaddo hutvā bodhiyaṃgaṇaṃ caṃkamitvā maddati  tadā thero vijānitvā etadavoca  
  
     bodhiyaṃgaṇaṃ susammaṭṭhaṃ disvā cittaṃ pasādayiṃ 
 pāpima  kissa mayhaṃ tvaṃ antarāyaṃ karissasi  
  
 māro therena ñāto ahaṃti ñatvā attānaṃ dassesi

 taṃ rūpaṃ daṭṭhumicchāmi  taṃ taṃ yācāmi pāpima

 sacce patiṭṭhito  vīra  adhiṭṭhānaṃ adhiṭṭhitaṃ     mettacitto tuvaṃ nātha  sukhadukkhe na iñjati

     pahūtajivhā rattoṭṭhā tassa sīhahanū subhā

 thero arahattappattoti jānitvā sakko devānamindo āgantvā yāci  gacchāma bhante devalokaṃti  thero gacchāma devānamindāti vatvā ekato gantvā sudhammāyaṃ sahāyaṃ devānaṃ tāvatiṃsānaṃ dhammaṃ desetvā iddhiyā devalokā āgantvā kālakandaravihāre aṭṭhāsi  tato aññataro nāgarājā sakabhavanā nikkhamitvā therassa santikaṃ gantvā teraṃ nimanteti pañcahi bhikkhusatehi saddhiṃ  thero adhivāsesi tuṇhībhāvena  taṃ yeva divasaṃ tambāyasumanatthero   therassa vandanatthāya āgato pañcahi bikkhusatehi saddhiṃ  so phussadevattheraṃ vanditvā āha  gacchāma bhante piṇḍapātassa kāloti  mā gacchatha  therehi ajja ekato piṇḍapātaṃ gaṇhissāmīti  adhivāsesi thero tuṇhībhāvena tato nāgarājā gantvā kālaṃ ārocesi  kālo bhanate piṇḍapātassa gamanāyāti nāgarājassa vacanaṃ sutvā phussadevatthera pamūkhā bhikkhusahassā  nāgarājassa  bhavanappadese nadītīre yathāvuddhaṃ ṭhitā  nāgarājā sapariso āgantvā therassa

 pattaṃ gahetvā dibbabhojanena pūretvā therassa adāsi dibbasāṭakayugaṃca  pādesu nikkhipi  thero taṃ piṇḍapātaṃ  sāṭakayugaṃ ca dutiyassa bhikkhuno adāsi  nāgarājā puna aññaṃ adāsi  thero tatiyassa bhikkhuno adāsi evaṃ  kamena sabbesaṃ sahassamattānaṃ  bhikkhūnaṃ dentassa dve bhikkhū tambāya āgatassa sumanattherassa sissā na gaṇhanti attano purato dinnameva gaṇhanti  taṃ disvā nāgarājā āgantvā te pucchi kissa bhante na gaṇhathāti  amhe mahārāja  vattabhedaṃ na karomāti  kiṃ  bhante vatta  bhedaṃti  sakalābhe santoso mahā rājāti  sādhu bhanteti vatvā dve sāṭakayugalāni dvinnaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ pādesu nikkhipi  tena nikkhittamatte tāni yugalāni cattāri yugalāni jātāni  taṃ disvā sabbe bhikkhū vimbhitā  nāgarājā pana anattamano te bhikkhū saṃvejetu kāmo phussadevattherassa guṇaṃ vaṇṇayanto āha  
  
     kāḷakandaravihāramhi phussadevo mahāvasī 
 bhattena taṃ nimantemi  tassa bhattaṃ dadāmahaṃ  
     thero paṭiggahetvāna yadi tumhaṃ na dassati  
 evaṃ thero na tumhākaṃ sukhatthi tu bhavissati  
     tassa therassa puññena demi bhattaṃ yugāni ca  
 thero paṭiggahetvāna sahassānaṃ dadāti hi  
     īdisaṃ sukataṃ puññaṃ pubbe aññāsu jātisu  
 taṃ puññaṃ natthi tumhākaṃ  paṭigaṇhātha paṇḍitā  
     mettāvihārī so bhikkhū arahā ca anāsavo 
 ete guṇā na tumhākaṃ paṭigaṇhātha paṇḍitā  
     imasmiṃ vanasaṇḍamhi santi pāṇā sudāruṇā 
 niccalohitamaṃsādā aññamaññavihesakā  
     tepi tāva   sukhaṃ laddhā theramettānukampato 
 hiṃsācittaṃ vivajjetvā aññamaññamaheṭhakā  
     īdiso guṇasampanno phussadevo mahāvasī 
 te guṇā natthi tumhākaṃ  paṭiggaṇhātha paṇḍitā

 eva manusuyyate  ariyavaradīpe anurādhapure aññataro kammārakamme cheko kammante visārado jāto  añññataro kasikammakārako kasiparikkhārāni kāretukāmo sālitaṇḍulaṃ sūkaramaṃsaṃ vettaggaṃ ca gahetvā tassa kammārassa paṇṇākāratthaṃ ānayi  so gahetvā cintesi  
  
    sālisūkaramaṃsaṃ me paṇṇākāratthamābhataṃ 
 paṇṇākārasahassānaṃ hetubhutaṃ karissahaṃ  
    etthantare ca cattāro bhikkhū piṇḍāya āgatā 
 anurādhapuraṃ  te va piyaṃgudīpavāsikā  
    evaṃ so cintayitvāna dakkhiṇeyye gavesati  
 gavesamāno kammāro addakkhi jinasāvake  
    tattheva te nimantetvā gharaṃ nesi vicakkhaṇo 
 āsane ca supaññatte nisīdāpesi bhikkhavo  
    sakkaccaṃ ca sahatthena pasanno tuṭṭhamānaso 
 sālimaṃsodanaṃ datvā paṇidhiṃ nikkhipī tadā 
    yaṃ yaṃ hi upapajjāmi dibbaṃ vā yadi mānusaṃ 
  paṇṇākārasahassāni upatiṭṭhantu  maṃ sadā 
    so taṃ dānaṃ varaṃ datvā arahantesu tādisu 
 teneva somanassena tahiṃ kālakato ahu  
    tattha kālakato santo sampatto  devikucchiyaṃ 
 duṭṭhagāmiṇirājassa puttattaṃ  so upāgato  
    gabbhe patiṭṭhamattena paṇṇākārā upaṭṭhitā 
 paṇṇākārasahassāni sā devī sampaṭicchati  
     gabbhā nikkhantamattassa kumārasseva denti te  
 paṇṇākārasahassāni anto tassūpapajjare  
  
 evaṃ paṇṇākārasahassāni paccupaṭṭhitāni dvādasavassāni honti  kumārassa jātiyā pabhuti sālisañcayo loke jāto hoti  tena sālikumārotissa nāma kataṃ  kālantare sālikumārassa bhariyā āsākamālinī nāma uttamarūpadharā caṇḍāladārikā hoti tassā ayaṃuppatti  
  
 atīte kāle kassapasammāsambuddhe parinibbute bārāṇasiyaṃ aññatarā duggatā mahallikā itthi saṃghassa ca dvinnaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ ca bhattāni deti  ekasmiṃ divase dve bhikkhū pageva tassā gharaṃ āgatā  upāsikā te disvā āha  na tāva bhante bhattakālo  yāva bhattaṃ samijjhati  tāva idha sālāyaṃ nisīdathāti  sādhūti te bhikkhū āsana sālaṃ gantvā dhammakathaṃ kathentā nisīdiṃsu  therikāpi khippameva bhattaṃ pacitvā dhītaramekaṃ pesesi  gaccha puttike  te bhikkhū ānehi ciraṃ te ṭhitāti  sādhu ammāti gantvā dhammakathaṃ katentānaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ pariyosānaṃ āgamayamānā dhammaṃ suṇantī aṭṭhāsi  sā gāthāpariyosānaṃ

     guḷamadhūphāṇitādi sakaṭasatehi pañcahi 
 ānītāni jānapadā kumārasseva kāraṇā  
 tepi sākaṭikā tatheva kumārasantike ṭhitā  sopi maṃ uddissa ānītānīti ñatvā sampaṭicchi  gharaṃ gantvā cintesi  nagarassa sāmantā yeva mama puññaṃ vipaccati  udāhu sakaladīpeti yaṃnūnāhaṃ vīmaṃseyyaṃti asoka māliniṃ rathaṃ āropetvā cetiyagiriṃ gato   cetiyagirissa ca gāmassa   ca antaraṃ patvā rathā oruyha kumāro bhumiyaṃ nisīditvā asokamāliniṃ evamāha  
  
  sl           
  
     chātosmi bhojanaṃ dehi  bhuñjissāmi idhevahaṃ  
 idha vanasmiṃ maggitvā khippaṃ ānaya sobhane  
 devī bhaṇati  
     nimmanusse araññamhi āhāro natthi sāmika  
 hatthesu natthi amhākaṃ dento  keci na vijjati  
     bhariyāya vacanaṃ sutvā adāsi kīḷadaṇḍakaṃ     
 etaṃ rukkhaṃ paharitvā dehi me bhojanaṃ bhaṇāti  
  
 sā sādhu sāmīti tiṭṭhadaṇḍakaṃ   gahetvā taṃ rukkhaṃ pahari bhojanaṃ dehīti daṇḍaṃ rukkhadevatāya kāyasmiṃ pati  taṃ disvā bhītā devatā evamāha  sāminī  kasmā maṃ pahari paṭhamameva mayā devatānaṃ tiyojanaṃ kataṃ bhattaṃ  sajjetha tumhe kumāro āgatoti  vatvā cattāro bhattakāje yakkhe harāpetvā pesesi  kumāro tāni disvā te yeva gāhāpetvā cetiyagiriṃ āharitvā bhikkhusaṃghassa  parivisitvā pacchā sayaṃ saha bhariyāya bhuñji   etena kamena satta divasaṃ cetiyagirimhi yeva nivuttho devatānaṃ upaṭṭhānena dānaṃ datvā anurādhapuraṃ paccāgato  rājā kumāraṃ disvā āha  
  
     tvaṃ me janapadaṃ gantvā pīḷetvāna mahājanaṃ 
 dhanadhaññaṃ vilumpetvā sabbaṃ raṭṭhaṃ vināsayi    
 kumāro bhaṇati  
     nāhaṃ deva vilumpāmi  devatā maṃ upaṭṭhitā 
 cetiyagirimhe vāhaṃ vutthomhi satta rattiyo 
     iti suci kusalo rājaputto 
 upacitapuññabalo balī bhavitvā 
 parijanapadajanappiyo   manāpo 
 visayasukhāni sadāva alattha  
     dasavidhakusalesu appamatto 
 bahuvidhadānapathe samaṃgibhuto 
 sugatigatipathaṃ visodhayitvā 
 sakabhavanaṃ viya yāti devalokaṃ  
  
  sl           
  
     catusampattipade katādhikāraṃ 
 idha ca parattha ca taṃ yathā kumāraṃ 
 amaragaṇā sadā piyā honti 
 kusalakarampi tathāvidhaṃ aññaṃti  
  
 sālikumārassa vatthu sattamaṃ       h k   ciraṃ karitvā     h k   dussate  
     k   kuṇḍalā     potthake katthi  
     k h   pamuccitvā      h k   suvaṇṇarūpakaṃsāni  
     h k   suddhānaṃ      k   janakāyā  
      a b   potthakesu natthi       a b   gāmagirissa  
      a b   tiṭṭhadaṇḍaka       k   devi daṇḍakaṃ 
     nippīletvā  lokappa       k   vinassati       k   parajanapada 
  
      saddhātissarañño vatthū   
  
 evamanusuyyate  sundaravaradīpe bahusādhujananilaye paramasubhikkhavati sīhaḷadīpe saddhātisso nāma rājā rajjaṃ kāresi  tassa rañño rahogatassa paṭisallīnassa vigatanīvaraṇa  cittassa sīhasayanagatassa evaṃ cetaso parivitakko udapādi   vuttaṃ hetaṃ bhagavatā saṃyuttanikāye devatāpañhe parisuddhadānaṃ vaṇṇentena  
  
    dadanti eke visame niviṭṭhā 
 chetvā vadhitvā atha socayitvā  
 sā dakkhiṇā assumukhā sadaṇḍā 
 samena dinnassa na agghametīti  
  
 yannūnāhaṃ aparampi paramaṃ visuddhaṃ dānaṃ mahānisaṃsaṃ dadeyyaṃ buddhappasatthaṃ kāyaparissamaṃ katvāti cintetvā deviyā nivedesi  
  
    sassakālo ayaṃ devī  sassāni phalitāni ca  
 saṃbhatikammaṃ karontā saddhā bhavanti  dāyakā   
    nivāsetvāna kāsāve gahetvā dhaññalāyakaṃ  
 sālikkhettāni gantvāna amma lāyāmi sālikaṃ  
    tāni sālīni ānetvā bhattaṃ katvā sabyañjanaṃ 
 saṃghato uddisitvāna ekaṃ bhikkhuṃ dadeyyahaṃ  
    yadi saṃghe dade dānaṃ  taṃ dānaṃ buddhavaṇṇitaṃ 
 dassāmi devi taṃ dānaṃ bhatikammaṃ karomahaṃ  
    tamatthaṃ deviyā vatvā kālasseva bahī gato 
 mahāpathe ṭhito gantvā pucchanto āgate jane   
    mahāpathe ṭhitaṃ disvā añño gahapatī naro 
 pucchati purato gantvā haṭṭhatuṭṭhena cetasā  
    sukhumālā karā pādā  sarīraṃ sukhavaḍḍhitaṃ  
 eko adutiyo samma  kissa tvaṃ idha tiṭṭhasi  
  
 rājā bhaṇati  
  
    kammakāro ahaṃ samma  karomi divasaṃ bhatiṃ  
 kammaṃ karitvā divasaṃ yaṃ labhāmi harāmi taṃ  
  
 gahapati bhaṇati  
  
     adiṭṭhapubbo ambhehi īdiso bhatiko naro 
 rājayoggo ayaṃ kāyo  bhatiyoggo na hotayaṃ 
  
 yo vā so vā hotu  khettaṃ lāyituṃ samatthosīti  rājā bhaṇati  āma samatthoti tena hi gacchāmāti taṃ ānīya khettaṃ dassesi  idaṃ me khettaṃ lunāhiti sādhū ti sampaṭicchitvā thāmavā rājā saddho ca sakaladivasaṃ kammamakāsi  tuṭṭho gahapati bhaṇati  samma  yattakaṃ sakkosi gaṇhituṃ tattakaṃ dhaññaṃ hara saha palālehīti  rājā sādhū ti vatvā mahantaṃ dhaññakalāpaṃ banditvā nikkhipitvā rattiyaṃ rājakulaṃ netvā antepure ṭhapesi  devī taṃ uṇhodakaṃ katvā sambāhetvā nahāpesi  tato dvepi janā dhaññaṃ madditvā  pālālaṃ uddharitvā dhaññaṃ aggahesuṃ  rājā deviṃ bhaṇati  
  
     devī imehi dhaññehi yaṃ kātabbaṃ karohi me 
 idha rājakulassanto mā yo koci pavīsatu  
     sādhūti sā paṭissutvā rājassa vacanaṃ kari 
 thusādiṃ kuṇḍakaṃ cāpi yathāmūlena vikkiṇi     
     guḷaṃ pūvaṃ ghataṃ sā ca sālikuṇḍaṃ manoramaṃ  
 tatheva sā samānesi dānakiccaṃ kataṃ mayā  
  
  sl           
  
     ekabhikkhussa sā bhikkhā  paṭiyattā tadā ahū  
 samānetvāna taṃ sabbaṃ rājā dāsiṃ idabravi  
     gaccha tvaṃ je ito khippaṃ bhikkhusaṃghassa santike 
 saṃghato uddisāpetvā   ekaṃ bhikkhuṃ samānaya  
     tassa vākyaṃ nisāmesi tissatthero mahavasī 
 piyaṃgudīpavāsī so dibbāya sotadhātuyā  
  
 sutvā thero aññataraṃ bhikkhuṃ āmantesi  eso āvuso tumhākaṃ upaṭṭhāko saddhātisso bhatikammaṃ katvā ekassa bhikkhussa atthāya piṇḍapātaṃ paṭiyādeti so ca taṃ saṃghassa  dātumicchanto  idāni dāsiṃ āṇāpeti bhikkhuṃ nimantetvā ānehī ti  dukkaraṃ āvuso raññā kataṃ taṃ piṇḍapātaṃ sampādentena  taṃ puthujjano mā paribhuñji  gacchāvuso tambapaṇṇidīpaṃ  tattha gantvā āsanasālaṃ pavisitvā yathāvuḍḍhaṃ tiṭṭha  tuyhaṃ pāpuṇissatīti  sādu bhanteti so bhikkhu vehāsaṃ abbhuggantvā tambapaṇṇidīpe otiṇṇo  otaritvā pattacīvaramādāya āsanasālaṃ pavisitvā yathāvuḍḍhaṃ aṭṭhāsi  rañño dāsī ārāmaṃ gantvā saṃghuddesakaṃ bhikkhuṃ pucchitvā taṃ bhikkhuṃ ṭhitikaṃ pāpuṇantaṃ nimantetvā ānesi  rājā ca devī ca paccuggantvā abhivādesuṃ  pattaṃ gahetvā rājā sajjita piṇḍapātena pūretvā sāṭakacumbaṭake pattaṃ ṭhapetvā paramanipaccākāraṃ katvā tassa bhikkhuno adāsi so bhikkhū piṇḍapātaṃ gahetvā evamāha  
  
     paripuṇṇamidaṃ dānaṃ ñatvā natthīti āsanaṃ 
 āsanaṃ alabhantohaṃ yena gacchāmi patthitaṃ  
     atippasādaṃ mākāsi  majjhatto hohi patthiva  
 atipītigataṃ cittaṃ sandhāretuṃ sudukkaraṃ  
     idaṃ vatvāna so bhikkhū pakkhirājāva ambare 
 khippaṃ gantvāna saṃghassa parivisī yathicchakaṃ  
     terasānaṃ  sahassānaṃ saṃpuṇṇaṃ āsi bhojanaṃ  
 dinnāvasesaṃ yaṃ atthi  attanā paribhuñji so  
  
  sl           
  
     dakkhiṇeyyaguṇaṃ disvā paccakkhaṃ paṭhavissaro 
 pasādaṃ vipulaṃ katvā pāpuṇi mānasaṃ   sukhaṃ  
 tato tassa rañño maraṇakāle upaṭṭhite dhammakathikā bhaṇanti  appamādaṃ karohi mahārāja  satiṃ paṭipajja  attano kusalaṃ anussarāhīti  rājā bhaṇati  
  
     suvaṇṇarūpā maṇimuttachāditā 
 dussāvikammaṃ mama kāritaṃ pure  
 dhamme ca saṃghe ca katādhikāro 
 bahuppakāro vipulo ahosi me  
     cātuddase paṇṇarase  yā ca pakkhassa aṭṭhamī  
 sīlāni guttāni surakkhitāni me 
 etāni sabbāni vihajja dissati 
 yamekabhikkhussa adāsi bhojanaṃ  
     iti narausabho narissaro so 
 naragaṇadevasamucchitārisaṃghe  
 ariyapurisapuggalassa datvā 
 tusitapurabhavanagatosi rājā      aparimitamanantamappameyyaṃ 
 paramasukhaṃ sukhadāyako alattha  
 ajarāmaramakkhayaṃ visokaṃ 
 labhatu no payaṃ dhammikova rājā  
  
 viceyyadānavatthu aṭṭhamaṃ  
 iti kaṇṭakasolapaṭṭanavatthabbena paṭṭakoṭṭi vihāravāsikena   ācariyadhammanandittherena kataṃ sīhaḷa vatthudasakaṃ tiṭṭhitaṃ  
  sl           
  
     mahādevaupāsakassa vatthu  
  
    dānānisaṃsavattāraṃ dānavatthujinaṃ budhā 
 dānā sambodhisampattaṃ dānavattānamuttamaṃ  
  
 ettha dānassa phalānisaṃso vatthunā saha saṃvavaṇṇito  kathetabbo  evamanusūyate  tambapaṇṇidīpe nissadanajanapade     vattagāmo  nāma ahosi tasmiṃ gāme mahādevo nāma upāsako paṭivasati  saddhopasanto dhammajīvī  so sassapāka kāle sampatte araññe khettassa sāmante tinakuṭikaṃ katvā rakkhituṃ nipanno  tato aḍḍharattasamaye aññataro peto annapānāni yācanto rodanto vilapanto mahāpathena gacchati  tassa saddaṃ sutvā mahādevo upāsako uṭṭhahitvā dūrato va paṭipucchi  
  
    ko nu rodati dukkhitaṃ  rattiṃ nimmānuse vane  
 annapānāni  yācanto vilapantova gacchasi  
 peto bhaṇati  
    ahaṃ hi samma petosmi  maccheravasamāgato  
 pāpakammaṃ karitvāna petalokamupāgato 
    abandhuko  anāthohaṃ natti me koci dāyako 
 ete sanāthā gacchanti bhutvā pītvā yathāsukhaṃ  
    hatthiassarāthādīhi yāyanti ca disodisaṃ  
 alaṃkārehi maṇḍetvā sanāthā  kāmakāmino  
    taṃ sutvāna mahādevo taṃ petaṃ etada bravi   
 kuhiṃ alatthuṃ   ete hi  kissa tvaṃ te nalabbhasi  
 peto bhaṇati  
  
  sl           
  
    dīpe rohaṇapassampi bodhipiṭṭhijanapade   
 annapānāni datvāna ñātipetāna muddisuṃ  
    te ñātipetā gantvāna anumoditvāna ekato 
 petabhāvaṃ jahitvāna dibbavaṇṇaṃ labhiṃsu te  
    te disvā paridevāmi rodāmi vilapāmi ca 
 piṭṭhito piṭṭhito yāmi yācamāno punappunaṃ  
 upāsako bhaṇati  
     vijahitvā manussattaṃ paralokaṃ gatā ca ye 
 tesaṃ uddissa dentī te   ñātakāpi añātakā  
 peto bhaṇati  
     aññātakā ñātakā vā uddisitvāna   denti ye 
 yadi petānumodanti  taṃ tesaṃ upakappati  
 upāsako bhaṇati  
     sādhu tvaṃ anumodāhi suve dānaṃ    dadāmahaṃ 
 sīlavante gharaṃ netvā annapānaṃ samuddisaṃ  
     anumodami taṃ samma  dehi me anukampaka  
 uddharehi apāyā maṃ  khuppīpāsāsamappitaṃ  
  
 tato mahādevo upāsako tassā rattiyā accayena vihāraṃ   gantvā adṭha bhikkhu nimantetvā purato gharaṃ gantvā sabbabhojanavikatikaṃ sajjetvā puna te bhikkhū ānetvā āsanesu nisīdāpetvā pāniyaṃ adāsi iminā vipākena petassa udakaṃ nibbattatūti uddisi  yāguṃ datvā kādanīyaṃ datvā bhojanīyaṃ datvā mālāpūjaṃ katvā iminā vipākena petassa  yāguādīnī    nibbattantūti uddisi  peto pi tattha anumoditvā dibbattabhāvaṃ paṭilabhi  bhikkhūpi bhuñjitvā anumoditvā pakkamiṃsu  upāsako 
  
  sl           
  
 punadivase khettaṃ gantvā nipajji  aḍḍharattasamaye so peto āgantvā pivitvā bhuṃjitvā maṇḍitvā dibbena rūpena upāsakassa avidūre ṭhito āha  
     uṭṭhehi samma  kiṃ sesi  passa sandiṭṭhikaṃ phalaṃ 
 sumittaṃ purisaṃ laddhā pattosmi paramaṃ sukhaṃ 
 upāsako tiṇakuṭiyā nikkhamitvā ṭhito taṃ petaṃ avoca  
     atidūre ṭhito samma  āgaccha mama santike  
 alaṃkataṃ taṃ passāmi  kissa lajjasi maṃ tuvaṃ  
 peto bhaṇati  
     lajjāmi samma  naggosmi  sāṭakaṃ natthi me pana  
 sabbāni paripuṇṇāni  ekaṃ me natthi sāṭakaṃ  
 upāsako bhaṇati 
     ekaṃ me sāṭakaṃ atthi  gaṇhāhi tvaṃ  dadāmahaṃ 
 taṃ sāṭakaṃ nivāsetvā āgaccha mama santikaṃ  
 peto bhaṇati  
     evaṃ dinnaṃ na me hoti sāṭakānaṃ satānipi 
 sīlavantesu yaṃ dinnaṃ taṃ petā paribhuñjareti  
  
 so tassā rattiyā accayena puna bhikkhū nimantetvā bhojetvā ekekassa bhikkhussa sāṭakayugaṃ datvā iminā vipākena petassa sāṭakāni nibbattantuti uddisi bhikkhū paribhuñjitvā gatā  puna upāsako khettakuṭikāya nipanno  peto devaputtarūpena aḍḍharattasamaye disā   obhāsetvā sabbālaṃkārabhusito dusse nivāsetvā āgantvā purato ṭhito āha  
  
     sammukhe purato ṭhatvā devaputto mahiddhiko 
 mahādevaṃ gahetvāna idaṃ vacanamabravi  
     mātāpitukataṃ netaṃ  ñātisālohitehi vā  yaṃ tumhehi kataṃ mayhaṃ tassa patikaromahaṃ  
  
  sl           
  
 so mahādevaṃ bāhāya gahetvā aññatarassa vaṭarukkhassa mūle netvā tisso nidhikumbhiyo dassesi  ekā suvaṇṇabharitā  ekā rajatabharitā  ekā kahāpaṇa bharitā imaṃ nidhiṃ gahetvā paribhuñjāhi ca parivārehi ca puññaṃ ca karohi mayhaṃ ca pattiṃ dehī ti vatvā sabba dhanaṃ tassa gharaṃ āharitvā ajeyyaṃ ca parehi katvā antaradhāyi   puna āha  
  
     sammā sabbaṃ vissajjetvā dātabbaṃ dānamuttamaṃ  
 pubbapete ca ārabbha atha vā mittadevatā  
     edisaṃ yo dade dānaṃ paccakkhaṃ labhate sukhaṃ 
 pecca sugatimaggena gacchate  neva tetaraṃ   
     tasmā ye  vuddhimicchinti attano  kāmakāmino 
 sumettā sīlasampannā atthakāmā hitesino 
 macecharaṃ pajahitvāna dāne abhiramantu te 
     mahādevo viya tepi bhavantu bahukā janā   
 sandiṭṭhikaphalaṃ bhutvā bhuñjante sugatiṃ puna  
     etādisāni sutvāna ñātipetāna muddisaṃ 
 dhammena dānaṃ dātabbaṃ dhammakāmena dhammikaṃ  
 mahādevatthu ekādasamaṃ 
  
      pāsāṇapetavatthu   
  
 eva manusuyyate  sīhaḷadīpe rohaṇajanapade saṭṭhimattā bhikkhū bodhiṃ vandanatthāya uttarāpathaṃ agamaṃsū  te anupubbena anurādhapuraṃ pavisitvā mahākoṇḍāya   mahātitthe   nāvaṃ abhiruhitvā kāveripaṭṭane  uttiṇṇā  tato kamena gacchantā mahāaṭaviṃ paviṭṭhātattha maggavimūḷhā jātā tattha bahunnaṃ hatthinaṃ gatamaggaṃ disvā maggoti maññamānā taṃ paṭipannā tīṇi divasāni 
  
  
     h b  dānavitthāramantakaṃ     h b   vattitāni  
    vatthugāmo  lokappa     ko nu kho āsi tvaṃ  samma 
  lokappa     pānaṃ hi  lokappa     aññātako  lokappa  
     a b k   rathāyuttā sivikā sandamānikā      k   kīḷantā 
     a b k   paribhāsati       k   alattha  lokappa  labhiṃsu  
      k   bodhipiṭṭhijanā bahū      kārenti  tīsūpi  
      lokappa  uddissa      a b k   svātanāya 
      a b   gharaṃ      k   alaṃkārādini  
     potthakesu natthi  
  
  sl           
 gantvā aññataraṃ mahantaṃ pāsāṇasadisaṃ ekakoppamāṇaṃ petaṃ disvā pāsāṇoti maññamānā āruhitvā nipannā  mahāthero pana uṭṭhahitvā bahi caṃkamanto hatthapāda sīsasaṇṭhānāni disvā peto ayaṃ  nāyaṃ pāsāṇoti ñatvā te bhikkhū pakkosi  ethāvuso  oruhatha peto ayaṃ na pāsāṇoti  te sabbe orūḷhā  peto sīsaṃ ukkhipi  taṃ disvā thero pucchi  
  
    ekakosappamāṇo te kāyo pāsāṇasannibho  
 ṭhānacaṃkamanaṃ natthi  kiṃ kammaṃ pakataṃ tayā  
 peto bhaṇati 
    petohamasmiṃ bhaddante  manussohaṃ pure ahuṃ 
 kassapasammāsambuddhe saṃghadabbavināsako   
    ārāmakhettavatthūni dhanadhaññāni sabbaso 
 yaṃ kiñci saṃghikaṃ dabbaṃ taṃ vināsemi dummati  
    evarūpāni dukkhāni tibbāni kaṭukāni ca 
 petaloke anubhutvā  pacchāviciṃ gamissahaṃ 
  
 mahāthero bhaṇati  kathaṃ tvaṃ samma saṃghikaṃ vināsesī ti  peto bhaṇati  
  
    parinibbute bhagavati kassape lokanāyake 
 saṃghassa khettato dhaññaṃ bhuttaṃ me saha ñātihi  
    puttadārā ca ñātī ca dāsakammakarā ca ye 
  sabbe samaggā bhuñjiṃsu dukkhaṃ bhuñjāmi  ekako  
    uḷāraṃ me kataṃ kammaṃ uḷāraṃ yeva dayhati  
 pipāsāpīḷito  mayhaṃ mukhe siñcatha pāniyaṃti  
  
 saṭṭhimattā te bhikkhū nadiṃ otaritvā patthi  pānīyaṃ āharitvā tassa mukhe āsiñciṃsu  paṭhamayāmato  paṭṭhāya yāva aruṇuggamanā ākirantānaṃ petassa jivhāpi na temeti  thero taṃ bhaṇati  bho kiñci assādaṃ laddhoti  peto bhaṇati  
  sl           
  
     yadi bhikkhusahassampi sattarattimpi me chupe  
 aggajivhā na temeyya  kuto kaṇṭhaṃ atikkame  
    edisaṃ kaṭukaṃ kammaṃ saṃghadabbavināsane 
 sukhaṃ idaṃti taṃ mantvā kataṃ me dukkhahetukaṃ  
     mayhameva  kataṃ kammaṃ mayhameva  vipaccati 
 vipaccamānaṃ taṃ kammaṃ  parittāṇaṃ na vijjati  
  
 bhaddantānaṃ sabbesaṃ siñcitaṃ udakaṃ yadi me galakaṃ atikkameyya imāya me gatiyā amutto bhaveyyaṃti sapathaṃ katvā bhikkhū pucchi ke pana tumihe āyasmanto kassa sāvakāti  mahāthero bhaṇati  
  
     sakyarājakule jāno jino gottena gotamo 
 somhākaṃ bhagavā satthā  tassa sissagaṇā mayaṃ 
 peto bhaṇati  
  
     gotamo yadi sambuddho uppanto lokanāyako 
 sattāhāke atikkante avīcigatiko ahaṃ  
     kassapassa ca buddhassa gotamassa ca satthuno etthantareyaṃ vasudhā vaḍḍhitā sattagāvutaṃ

 petaloke bahuṃ mayhaṃ bhuñjamānassa taṃ phalaṃ 
     idānavīciṃ gantvāna bhuttabbaṃ tassa sesakaṃ

     evaṃ dosāvahaṃ hoti saṃghasantakanāsanaṃ  
 guṇāvahampi vā tesaṃ ye taṃ rakkhanti sabbadā  
     tumihe tu gacchathedāni jālā jālenti me tanuṃ  
 maṃ disvā appamādena yuñjatha buddhasāsane  
     khaṇaṃ varaṃ labhitvāna lokasmiṃ yaṃ  sudullabhaṃ taṃ khaṇaṃ mā virādhetha yuñjatha buddhasāsane  
     paṭigacceva yuñjitvā dukkhassantaṃ karissatha 
 apāyaṃ duggatiṃ gantvā mā socittha yathā ahaṃ

      kasipetavatthu  
  
 eva manusuyyate  tambapaṇṇidīpe bahū bhikkhū bodhi vandanatthāya niggatā mahātoṇḍāya  nāvaṃ abhirūhitvā kāveripaṭṭane otiṇṇā  tato anupubbena gāmanigamarājadhāniyo atikkamitvā mahāaṭaviṃ sampattā  te

 sattadivasaṃ maggavimūḷhā parabbhamantā hatthiyūthagataṃ maggaṃ disvā taṃ paṭipannā  te tena gantvā aññataraṃ petaṃ mahantena naṅgalena balivadde yojetvā kasantaṃ disvā manussoti maññamānā yena so tena gatā  
 mahā thero avidure ṭhito maggaṃ paṭipucchi  
    sattarantindivaṃ sabbe maggamūḷhā bhavāmase 
 maggaṃ desehi bhikkhūnaṃ yadī jānāsi kassaka  peto bhaṇati  
    sattarattindivaṃ sabbe maggamūḷhā bhavantu te  
 ahaṃ anekavassāni maggamūḷehā bhavāmiti  
 thero bhaṇati  
    evaṃ sudīghamaddhānaṃ kena tvaṃ maggamohito  
 ko vā panettha samma tvaṃ  kiṃ vā kammaṃ kataṃ pure  
 peto bhaṇati  
    kāle kassapabuddhassa manussohaṃ tadā ahuṃ  
 mukhena pāpakaṃ katvā kasipetattimāgato  
    na pivāmi na bhuñjāmi  āsanaṃ sayanaṃ kuto  
 niccaṃ rattinditvā sohaṃ  kasanto ye va sañcariṃ  
    evaṃ mayhaṃ kasantassa kāyo jalati rattiyaṃ  
 yuganaṃgalagoṇā ca jalanti phālapājanaṃ  
    ḍayhamānassa kāyassa yamalokagatassa me 
 etthantareyaṃ vasudhā vaḍḍhitā sattagāvutaṃ  
    evaṃ bahūni vassāni dukkhaṃ kāyikamānasaṃ 
 anubhonto ca ḍayhāmi passa kammassa daḷhataṃ  
 thero bhaṇati  
    kīdisaṃ kaṭukaṃ kammaṃ kiṃ mukhena kataṃ tayā  
 tamahaṃ sotumicchāmi  saṃvegajananaṃ mama  
 peto bhaṇati

      sādhu sabbe samāgantvā suṇātha mama bhāsato  
 taṃ kammaṃ vyakarissāmi  yaṃ kammaṃ dukkataṃ mayā  
     addhānamhi atītamhi nagare kāsināmake 
 tattha rājā kikī nāma rajjaṃ kāresi pāṇinaṃ  
     tassa rañño adhiṭṭhānaṃ puraṃ bārāṇasī ahu  
 taṃ puraṃ upanissāya kassapo vasate jino 
     vassaṃ vasitvā bhagavā caramāno ca cārikaṃ 
 anukampamupādāya mama gāmaṃ upāgami  
     tasmiṃ gāme janā sabba saṃkaḍḍhitvāna  bhojanaṃ 
 kassapaṃ sugataṃ buddhaṃ nimantesuṃ sasāvakaṃ  
     ahaṃ ca tasmiṃ samaye pasunaṃgalaphālakaṃ 
 khandhe katvāna gacchāmi kasikammassa kāraṇā 
     maṃ disvā ñātako tatta atthakāmo hitesiko 
 mameva anukampāya idaṃ vacanamabravi  
     ayaṃ ca kassapo buddho āgato lokanāyako 
 taṃ yathāsattiṃ pūjenti kiṃ tvaṃ sammaṃ na pūjasi  
     sutvāna tassa vacanaṃ āghātetvāna mānasaṃ 
 abhāsitabbaṃ bhāsimhi aññāṇapakato ahaṃ  
     yadi ajja hi so buddho  mayhaṃ khettaṃ kasissati  
 evaṃ ahampi pūjeyyaṃ  kasi me nappavattati     
     etaṃ vākyaṃ udīretvā tattha kālakato ahaṃ 
 petalokaṃ idhāgantvā vedemi dukkhavedanaṃ  
     pattosmi īdisaṃ dukkhaṃ kaṭukaṃ ca mahattaraṃ 
 asidhārā mukhe yeva te dukkhā vipulā ahū  
     aguttavācaṃ  maṃ disvā saṃviggā hotha paṇḍitā 
 saṃviggamānasā hutvā muñcatha bhavadukkhato

     yo so dasabalopeto vesārajjavisārado 
 gottena gotamo nātho tassa sissagaṇā ime  
 peto bhaṇati

     yadi gotamasambuddho uppanno lokanāyako 
 sattāhake atikkante avīcigatiko ahaṃ

      taṇḍulapetavatthu  
  
 evamanusuyyate  tambapaṇṇidīpe cetiyagirimhi aññataro bhikkhu vasati sambahulehi saddhiṃ tassa bhikkhussa pitā cetiyagiriṃ āgato  so bhikkhu pitu bhattakāraṇā taṇḍulaṃ alabhanto ārāmikānaṃ hatthato saṃghasantakaṃ aḍḍhanāḷimattaṃ taṇḍulaṃ aggahesi sve dassāmī ti so tassā yeva rattiyā kālakato cetiyagirissa antare peto jāto  eko piṇḍacāriko bhikkhu taṃ maggaṃ aḍḍharattisamaye paṭipajjanto taṃ petaṃ jalamānaṃ ṭhitaṃ disvā paṭipucchi  
  
    sudīghakāyo duggandho aggikkhandhova dippasi  
 aṭṭhicammāvanaddhova  ko nu tvaṃ idha tiṭṭhasi  
    petohamasmi bhaddante dukkhito yamalokiko pāpakammaṃ karitvāna petalokaṃ idhāgato 
 thero bhaṇati  
  sl           
  
    kiṃ nu kāyena vācāya manā dukkataṃ kataṃ  
 kissa kammavipākena petalokaṃ idhāgato  
 peto bhaṇati  
    bhikkhu ahaṃ pure hutvā vasiṃ cetiyapabbate  
 pitussa me bhojanattaṃ taṇḍulaṃ pariyesayaṃ 
    na laddhaṃ pariyesitvā   tatorāmikahatthato  
 saṃghassa taṇḍulaṃ suddhaṃ  gahitaṃ aḍḍhanāḷikaṃ 
    sve nāḷiṃ paripūretvā dassāmīti manaṃ kataṃ 
 etissā rattiyā yeva kālaṃkatvā idhāgamiṃ  
 thero bhaṇati  
    etaṃ bhikkhuṃ pajānāmi  sīlavā so bahussuto 
 īdiso sīlasampannoso na gaccheyya duggatiṃ  
 peto bhaṇati  
    evaṃ so sīlasampanno sutavantopi sāsane 
 saṃghasantakaharaṇaṃ  accāsanne  vipaccati  
    yaṃ kiñci saṃghikaṃ bhaṇḍaṃ appaṃ vā nātimaññatha 
 vipākakāle taṃ kammaṃ vipulena vipaccati  
 thero bhaṇati  
     kittakaṃ kusalaṃ tuyhaṃ petalokā vimuttiyā 
 buddhe dhamme ca saṃghe ca tīsu pūjaṃ karomahaṃ  
 peto bhaṇati  
     girito yāva gāmaṃ hi gāvutattayaantare 
 sakaṭe sampayojetvā asaṃkiṇṇaṃ  nirantaraṃ 
     taṇḍulaṃ paripūretvā yadi saṃghassa dassatha  
 evāhaṃ parimuccāmi imāya petayoniyā  
     evaṃ vipulataṃ pattaṃ aḍḍhanāḷikataṇḍulaṃ  
 yadidaṃ na labhāpetha  mama muttī sudullabhā  
   
     h k   saṃghārāmika     saṃghassa sattakaṃ tassa  sabbesu  
     k   ajjhāpanne      k   abhinna ca

 tato thero pabhātāya rattiyā anurādhapuraṃ pavisitvā saddhātissarājassa purato aṭṭhāsi  rājā tassa pattaṃ gahetvā āgatapubbaṃ taṃ theraṃ pucchi  kiṃ bhante āgatatthāti  thero taṃ pavattiṃ ācikkhitvā payojanaṃ ācikkhanto taṇḍulatthāya mahārājāti āha  rājā kittakāti pucchi  thero yathāvuttameva ācikkhi  tato rājātīsu gāvutesu  sakaṭe ṭhapāpetvā taṇḍulehi pūrāpetvā bhikkhusaṃghassa adāsi  datvā petassa nibbattatūti uddisi  dinnamatte yeva so peto petattabhāvaṃ vijahitvā dibbarūpadhārī ahosi  puna rattiṃ thero taṃ maggaṃ paṭipanno  devaputto therassa vandanaṃ katvā purato añjaliṃ paggahetvā aṭṭhāsi  thero taṃ disvā pucchi

 vararucirābharaṇehi bhūsitaṃgo 
 varasurabhisugandhalimpitaṅgo

 ahaṃ vivaso  mamupāgato pure  
 maṃ amitadukkhasāgare  nimuggaṃ 
 atikaruṇāya yuto tvamuddharesi  
     parahitakarā bhavanti ye te 
 jinaparisā jinena vinītā bhavetha

 bhavatu ca sabbavimutti bhikkhunoti

      bhattantarāyakara petavatthu  
  
 evamanusuyyate  tambapaṇṇidīpe rohaṇajanapade pabbato nāma vihāre atthi  tatra mahābhikkhusaṃgho paṭivasati  tena kālena jānapadā manussā sahatthā dānāni dātukāmā vihāraṃ gantvā sabbaṃ bhikkhusaṃghaṃ timantenti  saṃghatthero sabbe bhikkhū nimantitā  vihāre bhattaṃ mā pacathāti ārāmike vāresi  taṃ ca vihāraṃ bhatta velāya sadā yeva piyaṃgudīpavāsī dve bhikkhū āgacchanti  te taṃ divasaṃ chinnabhattā jātā  saṃghatthero tattha kālaṃkatvā petaloke nibbatto  aññataro piṇḍapātacāriko bhikkhū bodhipiṭṭhijanapade araññe viharati mettāvihārī  so peto khuppipāsāparipīḷito aḍḍharattasamaye taṃ theraṃ upasaṃkamitvā vanditvā  avidūre  aṭṭhāsi  
  
 taṃ disvā thero pucchi  
    amanusso virūposi tava kāyo bhayānako 
 duggandho aṭṭhisaṃghāṭo  ko nu tvaṃ idha tiṭṭhasi  
 peto bhaṇati     āsi thero vihāresu  saṃghatthero vināyako  
 tumihe jānātha taṃ theraṃ  cavitvā so idhāgato  
 thero bhaṇati  
    etaṃ theraṃ pajānāmi  sīlavā so bahussuto 
 etādisānaṃ sādhūnaṃ duggati nūpapajjati   
 peto bhaṇati  
    evampi sīlasampanno sutaṃ atthi pi sāsane 
 ekavācāpadosena petalokaṃ gatova so  
 thero bhaṇati  
   
    uppajjati  sababesu  
  
  sl           
  
    vācādosuggirantassa yaṃ taṃ so tvaṃ  abhāsi me 
 taṃ vācādosaṃ akkhāhi sotumicchāmi taṃ tava  
    bodhipiṭṭhijanapade sabbe jānapadā janā 
 dānāni dātukāmā te sabbe bhikkhū nimantayuṃ 
    etaṃ disvāna so thero idaṃ ārāmike bravi  
 yadatthi     sabbabhikkhūnaṃ vihāre mā pacittha vo  
    ārāmikāpi taṃ sutvā na paviṃsu tadā tahiṃ 
 bhikkhū ca gocaragāmaṃ niggatā tena te pana  
    etaṃ vihāraṃ dve bhikkhū āgacchanti sadāva te 
 bhattaṃ bhutvāna gacchanti piyaṃgudīpavāsikā  
     acintetvāna so thero taṃ bhattaṃ paṭivārayi 
 āgantvā pana te bhikkhū chinnabhattā tadā ahuṃ  
     bhattantarāyaṃ katvāna bhikkhūnaṃ bhattakāminaṃ 
 khuppipāsāya ḍayhanto bhamāmi sabbato disā  
     yaṃ kiṃci saṃghikaṃ lābhaṃ appaṃ vā yadi vā bahuṃ 
 antarāyo na kātabbo ananto saṃghamāgato   
     ahaṃ apaccavekkhitvā abhāsiṃ antarāyikaṃ ekavācāpadosena dukkhaṃ pattosmi edisaṃ  
     mamaṃ disvā tuvaṃ bhante saṃvejetumarahasi 
 na vāreyya sutaṃ sīlaṃ taṃ kammaṃ mā vipaccatu   
 thero bhaṇati  
     kinnu tuyhaṃ karissāmi  muñcemi kena hetunā  
 buddhe dhamme ca saṃghe ca tīsu pūjaṃ karomahaṃ  
 peto bhaṇati  
     yadāyaṃ paṭhavī sabbā rohatī girisamantato 
 sakaṭānaṃ patho hoti  tadā mutto bhavissahaṃ  
     dukkhappattaṃ mamaṃ disvā gantvā desehi bhikkhunaṃ 
 carantu appamādena  bhāyantu saṃghasantakā  
     tassa petassa sutvāna taṃ hi so piṇḍapātiko 
 mahāvihāraṃ gantvāna vattamānaṃ adesayi  
  
     uppajjati  sabbesu      a b   yaṃ tisaso 
     k   parakāmitaṃ     h   saṃghadāmato 
     h   pāpapaccati  
  sl           
  
     tato sutvāna te bhikkhū bhītā saṃviggamānasā caranti appamādena saṃghalābhantarāyikā 
  
     īdisaṃ vyasanaṃ patto thero rohaṇapabbate taṃ sutvā dhammapītissa bhayaṃ jātaṃ anappakaṃ saṃghabhattantarāyakārakapetavatthu soḷasamaṃ 
      patākapetavatthu   
  
 evamanusuyyate  tambapaṇṇidīpe rohaṇajanapade dīghāvumahāthūpo ahosi  tassa patākā vātena ukkhittā kuṭumbiyassa sassagāmakkhette patitā  khettasāmiko khettapariyante āhiṇḍamāno taṃ passitvā gahetvā akkharāni disvāpi na chaḍḍesi  lobhacittena taṃ pārūpitvā pakkanto  so kālantarena kālaṃkatvā sahassaguṇaayopaṭṭāvaguṇṭhito peto hutvā nibbatto jalamānena kāyenāhiṇḍamāno bodhipiṭṭhijanapadaṃ gantvā aḍḍharatta samaye aññatarassa piṇḍapātikassa  samīpaṃ gantvā vatditvā  añjaliṃ katvā dūre aṭṭhāsi  taṃ disvā thero pucchi  
  
    sabbo kāyo paṭicchanno lohapaṭṭehi guṇṭhito 
 aggivaṇṇena sampanno ko nu tvaṃ idha tiṭṭhasi  
 peto bhaṇati  
    petohamasmi bhaddante ayopaṭṭehi guṇṭhito 
 satānaṃ dasapaṭṭāni ḍayhanto pārupiṃ sadā  
 thero bhaṇati  
    kiṃnu kāyena vācāya manasā dukkataṃ kataṃ 
 kissa kammavipākena ayopaṭṭena ḍayhasi  
 peto bhaṇati  
  
   
    idāni dipavāpithūpoti voharīyati  pubabe pana dighāvu kumārassa kāmaṃ gahetvā dīghāvuthūpoti voharitaṃti maññāmi  
  sl           
  
     ahaṃ manusso hutvāna  bahudhano kuṭumbiko 
 aneke katvā khettāni pekkhanto vicarāmahaṃ  
    dīghāvumahāthūpamhā patākā pavānāhaṭā 
 vātena gāvutaṃ gantvā  mama khette patiṭṭhitā  
    tattha patiṭṭhitaṃ disvā hatthena taṃ parāmasiṃ 
 pariyesanto passāmi akkharaṃ likhitaṃ tahiṃ  
    akkharānipi disvāna lobhacittenahaṃ tadā 
 gahetvā pārupiṃ tattha buddhathūpassa taṃ dhajaṃ  
    tato kālaṃ karitvāna petalokaṃ gato ahaṃ  
 ayopaṭṭāni vatthāni laddhā dasasatāni me     tāni paṭṭāni me kāyaṃ ḍahanti ayamaṇḍitaṃ  
 assādaṃ natthi me kiñci  bhusaṃ dukkhappavattiyā 
     āsanaṃ sayanaṃ  natthi annapānaṃ kuto mama  
 accantadukkhappattomhi  maraṇaṃ me na vijjati  
 thero bhaṇati  
     kiṃ kammaṃ  te karissāmi  mocemi kena hetunā  
 buddhe dhamme ca saṃghe ca dhajaṃ dassāmahaṃ tava  
     yadi vatthasahassānaṃ paṭākā āhaṭā idha 
  dīghāvuthūpe pūjeyya  evaṃ mutti bhavissati  
     iti vatvāna so peto tatthevantaradhāyatha  
 tato thero pabhātāya rattiyā sīghaso pana 
     paṭākā pariyesitvā laddhā paṇṇāsamattakā 
 dīghāvuthūpe pūjetvā  thero petassa uddisi    
  
 tassa nibbattatuti pattiṃ adāsi  tato puna rattiṃ āgantvā theraṃ evamāha  aṭṭhaṅgulamattaṃ me bhante matthakaṃ vivaṭaṃ  taṃ passāhiti  punadivase therena maggitvā paṇṇāsamattā labhitvā tatheva āropetvā pattiṃ adāsi tassa puna aṭṭhaṅgulappamāṇaṃ vivaṭaṃ  etena 
      h k   taṃ dhajaṃ pārupitvāna tattha kālakato ahaṃ

 devamanussasampattiṃ laddhā nibbāṇamāgatā

      balivaddapetavatthu   
  
 evamanusuyyate  tambapaṇṇidīpe ramanīye janapade vāmamanaddigāme  nadiṃ nissāya vihāro hoti  tasmiṃ vihāre aññataro piṇḍapātiko bhikkhu arahā khīṇāsavo gāmaṃ piṇḍāya pavisitvā garukakiccakaraṇāya  osakkanto addasa aññatarasmiṃ gumbantare ṭhitaṃ balivaddaṃ  disvā upasaṃkamitvā pucchi  
  
    gumbantaraṃ pavisitvā cirakālaṃ ṭhito asi  
 catuppadaṃ na phandeti  balivaddo va dissati  
 peto bhaṇati  
    petohamasmi bhaddante duggato yamalokiko 
 balivaddo bhavitvāna cirakālaṃ ṭhito idha  
 thero bhaṇati  
    kiṃ tayā pakataṃ pubbe yassa pāpassa hetunā 
 balivaddo bhavitvāna cirakālaṃ ṭhito tuvaṃ  
 peto bhaṇati  
    ahaṃ atītamaddhānaṃ ahosiṃ  gāmiko idha 
 anurādhapure pubbe tharukammaṃ      karomahaṃ  
    taṃkāle kassapo buddho uppanno lokanāyako  
 tassa buddhassa saddhammo dippate dīpalañjake  
    taṃ dīpaṃ upanissāya viharuṃ jinasāvakā  
 tesaṃ ca bhojanatthāya sālamekaṃ kariṃsu te  
    taṃ sālaṃ atipīḷetvā dhaññabījāni nikkhipiṃ  
 tāni bījāni sabbāni saṃvirūḷhānī sattahe 
    tattha  bījāni disvāna nappavisanti bhikkhavo  
 atikkantamhi sattāhe  mama khettesu ropitā  
    gāmakūṭo tadā hutvā bhikkhuparibhavaṃkaro 
 vāretvā āsanasālaṃ tesaṃ phāsuṃ nadāsa haṃ  
   
     h   vāmavanaddigāme      h   garukiccakaraṇāya 
     k h   garukakammaṃ kasimmaṃ     
  sl           
  
     etaṃ kammaṃ karitvāna  tattha kālakato ahaṃ 
 balivaddo  bhavitvāna petadukkhaṃ labhāmahaṃ  
     aphāsukaṃ karitvāna sīlavantānamīdisaṃ 
 phāsukaṃ natthi me kiñci sabbarattindivampi ca 
     kassapassa ca buddhassa gotamassa ca satthuno 
 etthantareyaṃ paṭhavī vaḍḍhitā sattagāvutaṃ  
     vassānaṃ gaṇanā saṃkhyā atikkantā bahū gatā 
 gacchato petalokaṃ me ṭhito kāyo vipaccati 
     pivāmi na bhuñjāmi  na nisajjā  na caṃkamo 
 hatthapādā na phandanti tiṭṭhatova sato mama  
     idānavīciṃ gantvāna bhottabbaṃ tassa sesakaṃ 
 pamādalobhajaṃ kammaṃ evaṃ taṃ vipulaṃ gataṃ  
     evaṃ dosāvahaṃ hoti aparādho guṇādhike 
 guṇāvahopi so hoti guṇavantesu tādisu  
     maṃ disvāna tuvaṃ bhante pasuṃ dukkhena ruppitaṃ 
 manussānaṃ nivedetha sādhūnaṃ bādhane phalaṃ  
     maṇḍape rukkhamūle vā sālāya sayanīghare 
 sādhūnaṃ vasanatthāya tattha pīḷaṃ na kāraye  
     sādhūnaṃ pīḷanaṃ katvā patvā petagatiṃ hi so 
 vedeti kaṭukaṃ dukkhaṃ yathā vedemahaṃ idha  
     saṃghaphāsuṃ karitvāna labhaṃ sugatiyā sukhaṃ 
 sabbadukkhakkhayo hoti dhammapītissa bhikkhuno  
 evaṃ so peto attano kammaṃ therassa nivedetvā sattadivasaṃ petattamhi ṭhatvā tattha kālaṃ karitvā avīcinirayaṃ paviṭṭho  
  
 balivaddapetavatthu aṭṭhārasamaṃ

      saṃghasantakapamattavatthu  
  
 evamanusuyyate  suraṭṭhajanapade sāhuthale  āḷārabālapaṭṭane porimāsiyā tīre koṇḍapūdivihāro  nāma hoti  tasmiṃ vihāre pāmokkho bhikkhū issariyavatāya taṃ vihāraṃ visamena paribhuñji  tassa maraṇakāle sampatte kharo vyādhi uppanno  taṃ vejjā disvā upaṭṭhāke nivārenti  imassa bhikkhuno pānīyaṃ mā detha  dinne vyādhi vaḍḍheyyāti  
  
 sādhūti vatvā upaṭṭhākā pānīyaṃ nādaṃsu  so aḍḍharattasamaye pānīyaṃ alabhamāno taṇhābhibhuto taṃ dukkhaṃ asahanto sayaṃ uṭṭhahitvā attano karakaṃ āmasi taṃ rittakaṃjātaṃ  ovarakā niggantvā paribhogaghaṭaṃ parāmasi tampi rittakaṃ jātaṃ tato gantvā pānīyacāṭiṃ parāmasi sāpi rittakā jātā  taḷākaṃ gantvā parāmasi tampi rittakaṃ jātaṃ tato gantvā porimāsinadiṃ passi sāpi rittakā jātā  taṃ nirūdakaṃ sukkhaṃ nadiṃ uttaritvā cintesi  mayhaṃ apuññavipākena sabbattha pānīyaṃ khīṇaṃ  avassaṃ mayā vacitvā petalokaṃ gantabbaṃ  idaṃ pubbanimittaṃ paccakkhaṃ mama dissati  pabhātāya rattiyā kathentassa me bhikkhū na saddahissantīti attano nahānasāṭikaṃ paratīrarukkhe bandhitvā puna otiṇṇo ovarake nipajji  so vibhātāya rattiyā bhikkhū āmante tvā sabbaṃ kathesi  
  
    idhāhaṃ āvuso rattiṃ pipāsādukkhapīḷito 
 taṃ dukkhamasahantova ālayā nikkhamiṃ tadā  
    ālayā nikkhamitvāna pāsito aḍḍharattiyaṃ 
 karakaṃ āmasitvāna na labhiṃ pāniyaṃ ahaṃ  
    tatheva paribhogāni pānīyacāṭiyo pi ca 
 āmaṭṭhamattakā sabbā rittakā parivattitā  
    bhinnaañjanavaṇṇābhaṃ sītalaṃ nimmalaṃ jalaṃ 
 dakapuṇṇataḷākāpi rittakā parivattitā  
      h   sāhuvale      a b   podimāsiyā     a b   koṇaḍacari  
  sl           
  
    acchā vālukasañjannā sabbakālampi sandati 
  porimāsī nadī vāpī  rittakā parivattitā  
    taṃ nadiṃ uttaritvāna tīre ṭhatvānahaṃ tadā 
 saṃviggamānaso hutvā evaṃ cintemi tāvado  
    aho acchariyaṃ kammaṃ kataṃ dukkavipākadaṃ 
 mayā  me pāpamāgamma paccakkhaṃ kammamīdisaṃ   
  
 bhikkhū na saddahanti  laggitaṃ sāṭakaṃ gahetvā ānetvā nikkaṃkhā bhavissatha  
  
    tassa taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā eko bhikkhū vicakkhaṇo taṃ nadiṃ uttaritvāna ānayī dakasāṭakaṃ  
    taṃ ca disvāna  te bhikkhū saṃviggamānasā ahuṃ  
 so bhikkhū  bhikkhūmajjhamhi idaṃ vākyaṃ udīrayī  
     bhavatī saṃghīkaṃ lābhaṃ appaṃ vā bahūkaṃ pi ca  
 tassa lābhassa sabbassa issariyaṃ kataṃ mayā  
     imassa ettakaṃ detha  asukassa ca ettakaṃ  
  thokaṃ detha bahuṃ detha mā dethāti nivārayiṃ  
     evaṃ issariyaṃ katvā datvāna saṃghasantakā 
 sacchandena pariccattaṃ yathā me sakasantakaṃ  
     mamaṃ disvāna sabbe te bhāyatha saṃghasantakā 
 bhāyitvā  appamādena ghaṭetha buddhasāsane  
     ghaṭetvā vāyamitvā ca bhāvetvā amataṃ padaṃ 
 dhammapītissa bhikkhussa piyaṃ dhammaṃ labhissathāti  
     evaṃ so attano dukkhaṃ nivedetvāna bhikkhunaṃ 
 tattha kālaṃ karitvāna petalokaṃ gato tadā  
  
 saṃghasantakapamattapetavatthu 
 ekunavīsatimaṃ

      taruṇabhikkhuvatthu   
  
 evamanusuyyate  susamiddhajanasamiddhe dhuvasassanipphattiyutte subhikkhubahule khamasukhanivāse  dasadisāvissutayase sabbakālaramanīye saddhaupāsakasaṇḍagaṇasevite suraṭṭhajanapade vissutagāme gāmavāsaṃ nissāya aññataro taruṇabhikkhu paṭivasati  pamādavihārī sakalarattiyā bhikkhūti nāmaṃ dhārento apaṭicchannakammanto pākaṭapadoso  ahu   evaṃ vasantassa tassa bhikkhuno bhariyā gabbhinī jātā  so taṃ gabbhaparipakkakāle vijāyanatthāya mātu gharaṃ hari  sā pana maggantare aññatarasmiṃ gumbantare vijātā  so taṃ lohitamakkhitaṃ duggandhiniṃ virūpabhūtaṃ disvā saṃviggo hutvā bhayabhīto paṭikkūlasaññaṃ uppādetvā cintesi

 rāgābhibhūto sammūḷho viparītena cetasā

    pariyattaṃ alaṃkatvāna pamādagamane mama 
 gahetvā puna pabbajjaṃ sampādessāmi sāsanaṃ

     idha   leṇe nikkhipitvā imaṃ posetha dārakaṃ 
 mahāvīro ayaṃ jhāyī jalabhiñño bhavissati

 bhikkhu therassa vacanaṃ sutvā dārakaṃ ovarake nikkhipitvā posesi  evaṃ so vaḍḍhamāno sattavassiko hutvā therassa santike pabbajitvā arahattaṃ sacchākāsi  chalabhiñño catupaṭisambhidāppatto  sabbaṃ ca buddhasāsanaṃ adhigami  so cittābhatthere   parinibbute bahunnaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ ācariyo hutvā yāvatāyukaṃ ṭhatvā parinibbāyi  so parinibbāṇasamaye sattatālaṃ vehāsaṃ abbhuggantvā antalikkhe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsi  
  
     buddhe dhamme ca saṃghe ca magge paṭipadāya ca 
 yassa ce saṃsayo atthi maṃ pucchatha yadicchatha  
     buddhe dhamme ca saṃghe ca magge paṭipadāya ca

     evaṃ svāhaṃ pabbajitvā jīvitaṃ kappemi sāsane

     k   cittaguttherassa      k   etha       k   cittagutthere

     pamādena vasantassa bhariyā me gabbhinī ahū  
 disvā vijāyamānaṃ taṃ jātaṃ me kāmato bhayaṃ  
     tena saṃsārabhītohaṃ   gacchiṃ cittābhapabbataṃ   
 puna me pabbajantassa araññeva rato mano  
     tattha kālaṃ karitvāna hutvāna opapātiko

     saṃvejanīye saṃvego edisova mahapphalo  tasmā lokavidū buddho vaṇṇito dullabho iti  
     evaṃ so ariyo thero nisīditvāna ambare 
 kammaṃ kammavipākaṃ ca pakāsesi sayaṃkataṃ
